Japanese Side Drafts Yet Another Economic Cooperation Plan 80

The Japanese Economic Investigation Group in Peiping Formulates a So-Called Cooperation Plan Which Has Already Arrived in Peiping

Beiping Correspondence: Japan is now drafting a new plan for the development of North China's economy. Experts from the South Manchuria Railway Company, representatives from the Japanese military, and representatives from the puppet regime's business community are establishing a "North China Economic Investigation Group" in Beiping. The group is organized into five sections: (1) Railways, (2) Highways, (3) Mining, (4) Port Construction, and (5) Commerce. Nonaka, the director of the 6th section of the Economic Investigation Committee who came to Beiping the other day, has already returned to Dalian to report. After a concrete plan has been drafted, Nonaka will come to Beiping again to organize the "North China Economic Investigation Group". Regarding the issue of Sino-Japanese economic cooperation, Foreign Minister Hirota repeatedly proposed it to Chiang Tso-pin, the Chinese ambassador to Japan, before Chiang returned to China. The Japanese side has already sent the Sino-Japanese economic cooperation plan to Beiping, the contents of which are as follows:

Sino-Japanese economic cooperation must fundamentally improve China's national economy. The main points are as follows: (1) In agriculture, accept Japanese technical guidance, with the goal of increasing the utility value of agricultural products for Japanese industry. (2) Develop mining, with cooperation in both capital and technology. (3) Technological and capital cooperation in the development of transportation. (4) Cooperation in the textile industry and other industries. (5) Establish a Sino-Japanese Trade Agreement Association to promote civilian interaction. (6) Revise Chinese tariffs to restore the Sino-Japanese Agreed Tariff Rates.

Agriculture

Agriculture is the foundation of China's national economy, with an annual production value of about 1.5 billion yuan. Japanese technical assistance could increase income and help alleviate China's international balance of payments imbalances. (1) Encourage cotton planting and provide technical assistance to make China one of the world's three major cotton producing countries. Japan imports about 200 million yuan worth of cotton annually. However, knowledge of cotton planting is rudimentary and requires Japanese technical assistance to improve quality, so that Chinese rural villages and the Japanese textile industry can achieve a policy of co-existence and co-prosperity. (A) China's encouragement of cotton planting and the possibility of Chinese cotton exports: China's cotton production has recently been about 10 million dan annually, with a consumption of 9 million dan. Due to quality reasons, it still needs to import 2 million dan from foreign countries annually. Currently, the National Government is expanding cotton growing areas to 60 million mu (currently 40 million mu) based on the cotton encouragement plan. This would allow for a harvest of 14 million dan, meeting the consumption of 10 million dan, with a surplus of 4 million dan. However, based on the quality of current products, foreign cotton may still need to be imported for two or three years. If China raises cotton import taxes or cancels export taxes, then Chinese cotton exports will not be difficult. (B) The Japanese side's facilities for improving cotton: Japanese textile operators in China have already achieved considerable success in lending excellent cotton seeds and improving cotton quality in Shandong, Henan, Hubei, and other provinces. Recently, a certain party has completed a survey for planting cotton along the Beining Railway Line and is implementing part of it. (C) A cotton planting salvation movement: In North China, a unique policy of national industrialization is being pursued. Due to the low profits from planting wheat and soybeans, there is a shift to planting profitable cotton, the so-called "cotton planting salvation movement". (2) Planting wheat: China is the world's second largest wheat producer, but imports 10 million yuan of wheat annually. Japan needs to import 70 million yuan from Canada, the United States, and Australia every year. Japan is recognized worldwide for its superior wheat cultivation and can provide technical guidance to China. (3) Wool: Recently, Japan's domestic wool weaving industry has developed, and the demand for wool has increased sharply. Japan needs 1.8 million dan every year, mostly from foreign countries. China's wool production has not been accurately counted, but it was roughly 250,000 tons last year, mostly exported to the United States. Japan only imported 12,000 dan. In the future, China and Japan should work together to increase China's wool production. (4) Other technical guidance: Improving agricultural fields and training rural instructors is necessary. The ten counties of Luan Dong in China have always relied on Japan. Through the introduction of a certain party, instructors have been dispatched to intern at the South Manchuria Railway Agricultural Experiment Station. In addition, the Japanese side provides guidance on water irrigation projects. Research on the industrial utilization of agricultural raw materials such as cotton and wheat, besides the raw materials needed by Japan, such as vegetable oil and pig bristles, can provide raw materials for industrial countries. "Implementing a group economy" means that neighboring countries have a prior obligation to supply.

Mining

(1) Iron: Daye and Elephant Trunk Mountain in Hubei, Taozhong in Anhui, and Jinlingzhen in Shandong already have relations with Japan. In addition, Japanese technical cooperation and capital cooperation are necessary for iron ore in provinces such as Chahar, Henan, and Fujian. (2) Antimony and Tungsten: Refining is necessary for antimony in Hunan and tungsten in Guangxi, and Japan must provide guidance. (3) Oil: Japan can provide lessons for oil field surveys in Shaanxi. (4) Coal: Coal is most suitable for Sino-Japanese barter trade. Japan should provide capital and technical assistance to Shanxi, Shaanxi, and Henan.

Transportation

China's railways are underdeveloped, making it very difficult to transport products from the interior to ports. Shanxi's coal and Henan's cotton would be much more active if there were railways directly to the seaports. Japan has plans to extend the Jiaoji Railway and build the Cangshi Railway for transportation.

Textile

It is well known that China's textile industry is depressed, and therefore, it needs Japan's rescue. Recently, there has been a trend of high-end products being transported to Japanese textile factories. This is not necessarily detrimental to Japan. The key is how the parties cooperate.

In order to promote close Sino-Japanese economic relations, and especially to promote civilian, spiritual, technical, and capital approaches to Sino-Japanese trade, a "Sino-Japanese Trade Agreement Association" should be organized, following the example of the Japanese-American and British-Japanese trade agreement associations. Moreover, the Sino-Japanese tax rates set in May of the 8th year of Showa (1933) expired, and Japanese cotton textiles, seafood, wheat, etc. lost preferential treatment. China's cotton, embroidery, and silk fabrics also lost special rights. The tax rate on Japanese goods was raised by 20% to 80%, or even as high as 150% to 600%. No matter how one explains it, the result is strongly anti-Japanese. Japan is urging China to wake up. As a result, last July, the Japanese side requested a revision of the tax rates. The tax rate on seafood was lowered, and the tax rate on cotton textiles was reduced very little. The Japanese side was ultimately dissatisfied. Recently, China again increased all import taxes, but exempted export taxes and transit taxes. If Sino-Japanese economic cooperation is implemented, improvements should be made. (20th)

Bandit Atmosphere Rampant in Luan Dong 81

Large and Small Bands of Bandits Are Everywhere; Liu Guitang and Shi Yousan Are Up to No Good

Tianjin Correspondence: Recently, the bandit atmosphere near the Great Wall Line has become rampant. Villages and towns in the northern borders of Zunhua, Qian'an, Miyun, and Xinglong counties are particularly areas where bandits roam. Due to the growing green crops, the bandits' tracks are elusive and uncertain, making it difficult for the security teams to encircle and suppress them. Recently, a band of over 700 bandits led by Ma Huwu from Dongjia Flavor occupied the area and planned to infiltrate from inside Malan Pass, harassing Zunhua and Jixian counties. The bandit gangs were organized like the military, calling themselves the pseudo-North China Autonomous National Salvation Army, and were organized into 37 detachments. However, the Japanese and puppet troops in Malanyu were heavily guarded. The bandit gangs only stayed in Dongjiakou and did not actually disturb the interior. In Zunhua, Lulong, and Qian'an, the people are panicking. The county towns have conscripted large groups of militia to defend the city, closing the city gates tightly during the day and inspecting suspicious individuals. County Magistrate Li of Xinglong specifically went to Tangshan on the 17th to meet with Yin Rugeng and pleaded for the security team to be dispatched to suppress the bandits. On the 16th, about 500 bandits from the pseudo-North China Army led by Li Laobao were discovered near the Great Wall Line at Tiemenguan and Fouerling near Shanhai Shimensai. The Zhang Yantian Division of the Second Security Corps rushed to encircle and suppress them. The bandits relied on the mountain's dangers to resist, and after a fierce battle lasting one day and night, the bandits were finally unable to hold out and fled to the vicinity of Xifengkou on the morning of the 17th. The area has been placed under special alert. However, there are many lurking bandit gangs east of the Shi River and around Shanhaiguan, all hidden in the green crops, and they are active at night, causing unrest around Yuguan. Gunfire occurs from time to time at night, and residents cannot sleep peacefully. The police of the Shanhaiguan Special Public Security Bureau and the police of Linyu County can only maintain the city gates and are unable to go out of the city to search and suppress the bandits. Therefore, the area three or four li away from the city is within the bandits' sphere of influence. In Xituogu Village, west of Beimaguan in Miyun, there is a traitorous civilian named Peng Ziyun, who is nearly sixty years old. Recently, he has been very active, gathering more than 500 bandits, organizing a pseudo-army, issuing blue cloth military uniforms to each person, and wearing yellow armbands, calling themselves the North China Army. He intends to contact the bandit gangs at various passes along the Great Wall and carry out a major operation. The county magistrate of Miyun has reported to the Jiji District Administrative Commissioner's Office and requested that the security team be sent to suppress the bandits, so as to prevent the bandit forces from spreading. In addition, a gang of about 200 mounted bandits, armed with well-equipped firearms, recently appeared near Shixia, Miyun. They came from Yanqing in eastern Chahar. On the 16th, they fought fiercely with the security team in Xiahe Village for one night. The bandits abandoned more than a dozen corpses and fled to Xiachengzi. Before leaving, they kidnapped more than a dozen men and women. There is also a bandit gang entrenched on Zhongfeng Mountain in western Miyun, with a population of about 600 to 700. All the villages in the vicinity have been looted, and they intend to invade the county seat. Wang Boling, the county magistrate of Miyun, specifically invited all the gentry of the county on the 17th to discuss the city defense methods and decided to conscript strong men from various villages to organize temporary militias and assist in the defense separately. The above is only the largest and most disruptive bandit gangs. Robberies, arson, and killings by sporadic small gangs in other counties are everywhere. Yin Rugeng has scheduled a visit to various counties in late August to provide instructions on joint defense methods. It has been found that the rampant bandits in the war zone are instigated by Liu Guitang and Shi Yousan, creating chaos and doing evil in the process. Therefore, suppression is not as simple as dealing with the bandits themselves. (19th)

Beiping's Treacherous Merchants Smuggling Silver Repeatedly 82

The Inside Story of Fresh-Faced People Transporting Silver Out of the Pass; Several Treacherous Merchant Organizations Uncovered

Beiping Correspondence: Since the occurrence of the silver dollar problem in Beiping, the amount of silver dollars flowing out has not affected the cash reserves of the various banks. However, it is feared that the silver dollars transferred to Beiping from other ports in the past six months have all been secretly transported out of the country by a group of treacherous merchants. Looking at the daily Ping-Shen through train between Ping and Yu, there are about fifty or sixty fresh-faced passengers, or even more than one hundred, carrying a suitcase each. Counting on the basis of each person carrying 400 yuan of silver, the amount of silver flowing out in the past six months can be seen.

The Beiping authorities have considered the method of preventing the outflow of silver dollars again and again. In addition to writing to the Japanese side requesting them to assist in cracking down on fresh-faced people who privately transport silver dollars, they are also paying attention to the collusion of treacherous merchants. Over the past few months, these treacherous merchants have had three burrows for cunning rabbits and used very sophisticated tactics, so their secret organizations have not been uncovered. According to inquiries from various sources, the batches of fresh-faced people who constantly travel back and forth smuggling silver are entirely hired by treacherous merchants. Generally, the profit earned for every 100 yuan is split in half, 4-6, or 3-7, depending on the market price. The profits earned by these treacherous merchants in the past six months are almost uncountable.

The Police Department of the Japanese Embassy in Beiping has repeatedly detained fresh-faced people carrying silver dollars at the East Railway Station and Xizhimen Railway Station. Although the number has not been counted, it is believed that it is definitely not small. On the surface, it is a loss to the fresh-faced people, but in reality, it is purely a sacrifice by a group of treacherous merchants. Therefore, no matter how much is intercepted, it is of no interest to the smuggling fresh-faced people. Although the Japanese have been very generous in their handling of the intercepted silver dollars, distributing them to various banks with paper currency issuance, the amount is only a drop in the bucket. However, this may alert the treacherous merchants that employing fresh-faced people is not reliable.

Recently, the Ping-Shen train encountered bandits near the Shi River, and all the paper money received by the fresh-faced people outside the pass was robbed, which must have dealt a not insignificant blow to the treacherous merchants. According to transportation industry news, in the past week, the number of fresh-faced passengers on the various trains between Ping and Yu has suddenly decreased, and it is believed that the number of fresh-faced passengers carrying silver dollars has also sharply decreased. According to financial industry news, in the past week, there has been no significant change in the silver dollars in Beiping. The amount of silver deposits has been slightly increasing every day. This proves that there has been no outflow recently. One of the reasons why silver deposits can be stabilized is that the private transportation by fresh-faced people has decreased. However, the recent breaking of smuggling organizations in Ping has an important relationship.

The situation of the Ping Municipal Public Security Bureau's detective team breaking private silver dollar organizations in recent days is briefly recorded as follows: (1) On August 16, the first detective team discovered in Tiande Zuo cigarette shop on Meishi Street outside Qianmen that the shop manager, Mu Ziyuan, secretly purchased silver dollars and transported them out of the country to make profits. Mu Ziyuan and the shop assistant, Wan Ruiqing, were arrested. According to their confessions, Liu Ziming, the main culprit, was arrested at No. 19 Caijia Hutong, and more than 1,000 silver dollars and multiple silver-transporting vests were found. Liu confessed that he had been operating this illegal incident for two months, transporting out 2,000 to 3,000 yuan every day. (2) On the 17th, plainclothes police arrested Zhang Yupei, the shopkeeper of Wang Chengxiang cigarette shop at No. 90 North Road, Tianqiao, and Guo Zongwen, the shopkeeper of Guo Ji cigarette shop, and several bags of silver dollars. In addition, Rao Yingge, a resident of No. 40 Sunjia Pit, Longfusi, Dongcheng, was discovered by Li Tonghui, a policeman in the Third District, selling silver dollars, and was arrested on the evening of the 17th and confessed without denial. (3) On the 18th, when the Yiji Money Shop in the Meat Market was engaged in private silver dollar smuggling, the detective team of the first detective team went to search and seized Liu Baotian, Ma De, Li Yu, Li Jinbo, He Yongxian, Liu Shaoming, and other criminals involved in buying and selling silver dollars. More than 500 silver dollars were found on each person. (4) According to news released by the detective organization, in addition to breaking the above-mentioned private transportation organizations in recent days, He Xing and Xin Maosheng cigarette shops, and Yisheng and Ding Taichang grain shops were also discovered to be smuggling silver dollars. They were searched one after another, and many people were arrested. The total amount of silver dollars found was over 10,000 yuan.

The authorities attach great importance to the handling of the key criminals involved in smuggling silver dollars that have been broken up in recent days and have decided to punish them in accordance with the Central Government's specially promulgated orders and the laws of the Republic of China for endangering the country. Therefore, those with serious circumstances will be sentenced to death to warn against illegal practices. (20th)

Anhui Province Intensifies Flood Prevention; Survey and Repair the Sui River to Unblock the River 83

Wuhu Correspondence: After the Yellow River breached in Shandong Province and the main flow invaded south, the Anhui Provincial Government ordered Lu Peizhang and Nan Yuejun, the commissioners of the sixth and seventh districts of northern Anhui, to summon the county magistrates to hold a meeting to discuss measures to defend against the Yellow River water and ordered the relevant dikes to be repaired completely to prevent emergencies. It also sent personnel to inspect and supervise. Now, the provincial government has received successive reports from the relevant county governments and Cui Bingsen, the commissioner sent, that the Yellow River flood has passed Shaanxi Province, and the water situation in Weishan Lake in Jiangsu Province increased by an average of about two inches from the 1st to the 6th of this month. After the 6th, it gradually eased, but on the 10th, the area around the lake increased by more than two inches, and the situation gradually became serious. The provincial government is deeply concerned that the Yellow River breach in Henan Province will cause the main flow to turn sharply downward, and it has telegraphed the Suxian County Government to inform the relevant counties to strictly prevent it in accordance with successive telegrams. It also ordered the situation of the defense of the various counties in northern Jiangsu after the Yellow River entered the Central Canal to be reported for investigation. In addition, the provincial government believes that the various rivers in northern Anhui, which are close to Jiangsu and Henan, have been repaired well in recent years, and the river dikes are also very strong, but the Sui River still needs to be repaired urgently. The river was previously surveyed and completed by a joint measurement team composed of the provincial governments of this province and Jiangsu Province and the Huai River Guidance Committee. The provincial government also intends to send personnel to survey and handle it immediately and supervise Suxian to convene an emergency meeting to repair the river dikes in order to ensure that the river dikes are strong and the river is unblocked to prevent floods. (20th)

Songjiang: The Shenhu Ferry Robbery Case Solved 84

The robbery and assault on the Shenhu ferry last month in Songjiang County, in which an old man was injured, was reported to the land and water public security agencies for investigation, but no news was received. Recently, Yang Shijie, the captain of the Public Security Bureau's detective team, learned that a certain Fang was among the bandits in this case, residing in Litahui Township. He sent someone to secretly investigate. When Fang's wife fell ill and returned home, she came to Songjiang yesterday to buy things. Captain Yang, based on a tip-off, went to Dacang Bridge with detective Shen Guichang to meet Fang and arrested him. When questioned, he said his name was Fang Ziguang, and he was being escorted back to the county bureau. While passing through Xita Lane, the thief remained expressionless and ran away in the lane. Yang and others chased after him and captured him in a paddy field. After taking him to the bureau for interrogation, he confessed without denial. A pawn ticket was found and checked at the Yifeng pawnshop. It was a Huchou silk fabric and was indeed one of the stolen goods from the ferry. The clothes he was wearing were also stolen goods sewn by hired workers. Based on the confession, Yang and others heard that another thief had been captured in Ganxiang, and there were still bandits at large. They are buying leads and tracking them down separately.

Changshu: North-South Trade Opposes Increased Business Tax 92

The local native goods industry is currently facing sluggish business and is in a state of depression. The industry believes that the existing tax burden of 2,000 yuan is already too heavy, and it will be impossible to bear any further increase. Therefore, Wang Mengsheng has been designated as a representative to request a reduction from the Business Tax Bureau, with the minimum requirement that there should be no increase. However, this has not been approved, and the industry is extremely indignant and plans to follow the rice industry's example by staging a complete strike to resist. The Chamber of Commerce and other organizations are currently mediating.

Zhenjiang: Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce Asks Songyun Office to Revoke Punishments for Various Soy Sauce Workshops 93

The Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a telegram to the Songjiang Salt Transport Commissioner's Office, stating that Song Junjian, Deputy Salt Transport Commissioner of Songjiang, had received a submission from Liu Zhuoyun, Chairman of the Zhenjiang Soy Sauce Industry Association, and five soy sauce industry representatives, including Zhou Shoutian, Tan Jingru, Zhang Xingru, Zhao Huiqing, Cai Fengxiang, and Liu Huanzhang, stating that they had received a letter from the Zhenjiang Zhejiang Salt Main Depot, forwarding a letter from the Zhejiang West Su Five Prefecture Salt Merchants Association, forwarding Instruction No. 1604 from the Songjiang Salt Transport Deputy Commissioner's Office, which stated: "According to an investigation, the Su Five Prefecture monitoring stations have reported in the soy sauce sales lists for the 23rd year that soy sauce workshops in Yixing, Jintan, and Liyang counties did not receive official salt throughout the year, and soy sauce workshops in Zhenjiang County received excessive amounts of official salt. It is suspected that there are cases of privately increasing vat openings and purchasing illicit salt. The office dispatched Ling Xichao, Chief of the Sixth District of the Su Five Prefecture Tax Police, Liu Shengqi, a clerk from the Songjiang Branch, and Ding Shiding, a clerk from this office, to conduct a thorough investigation after April 30 this year. Now, according to the report from the said officials, the actual situation has been investigated, and measures for suppression and correction have been drafted. We request that these measures be reviewed and implemented, and the investigation report on the vat openings of each soy sauce workshop, the table of salt consumption by soy sauce workshops, the table of refined salt used for soy sauce production by soy sauce workshops, and various vat opening documents are attached. It has been found that the names and garden names of most of the soy sauce workshops in Zhenjiang do not match the licenses, indicating that they are operating under borrowed licenses, using large vats and refined salt for soy sauce production, and privately increasing vat openings. These are serious violations of the regulations and damage to tax revenue. As for the soy sauce workshops in Yixing and Liyang counties, although the violations are less serious, they are still illegal. Based on the report, in addition to submitting the proposed suppression and correction measures to the department for review and implementation and issuing public notices separately, we will also determine the supplementary donations and fines and the revocation of licenses in accordance with Articles 2 and 3 of the Soy Sauce Workshop Suppression Regulations. We order the association to comply immediately, relay the instructions to the soy sauce workshops in each area, and promptly prepare the vat donation fines and the original licenses according to the list and submit them to the office within half a month for verification and handling, without any delay. Furthermore, any soy sauce workshops found operating without a license will be severely punished. We also order you to publicize and comply with these instructions. This is extremely important." Another Instruction No. 1690 from the Songjiang Hall Transport Deputy Commissioner's Office stated: "An investigation has revealed that the soy sauce workshops in Zhenjiang, Yixing, and Liyang are operating under borrowed licenses and have privately increased vat openings. This office has previously dispatched personnel to conduct further investigations and has determined the supplementary donations and punishments. On June 29 this year, Instruction No. 1604 was issued to the association, ordering compliance. Now, more than a month has passed, and no report has been received. What are the merchants Hengchang and Zhang Yiyuan doing? This is extremely dilatory. We hereby issue another order urging you to comply immediately, relay the instructions to the soy sauce workshops, order them to prepare the vat donation fines and the original licenses according to the list, and submit them to the office by August 15 for verification and handling. If there is any further delay or hesitation, the police will be instructed to enforce the order against each household according to the list, or revoke the licenses and order them to cease operations, as a warning. The merchants Zhang Hengchang and Zhang Yiyuan, who are responsible for guaranteeing compliance but have failed to do so despite repeated urging, shall be held jointly liable and ordered to pay the vat donation fines. Consider this a warning. Also, publicize this knowledge without delay. This is extremely important." Copies of the Soy Sauce Workshop Suppression Regulations are attached. How are the regulations stipulated? Since there has been no clear notification and salt has been purchased repeatedly, the depot has never refused due to discrepancies in the licenses and has never provided guidance. Therefore, since the fourth year of Tongzhi in the Qing Dynasty until now, more than seventy years have passed, and there have been countless mergers and transfers. This has become a habit. The vat licenses are obtained by the depot on behalf of the workshops. Recently, due to doubts about the amount of donations, we have truthfully presented our plight and requested that the old licenses be exempted from revocation and the punishment be revoked. However, we believe that requiring soy sauce workshops to obtain vat licenses is only a special measure in Su Wu Prefecture and Zhejiang Province, and no other provinces have such a special prohibition. Even Yangzhou, which is nearby, does not have it. Recently, since soy sauce has been sold throughout the country, soy sauce made in areas where the tax rates on Huai salt are lighter has been shipped to Zhenjiang in full loads. The business of merchants has been greatly affected. As leaders of the merchants, we are more familiar with the situation and should be more concerned. Therefore, we have jointly appealed to you, requesting that the chairman review the situation and allow us to present the difficulties of the merchants to avoid innocent people being punished and harming their business." Based on this, we believe that the suffering described by the merchants is real. The market has been depressed in recent years, and business has been slow. If we apply the regulations, it will be difficult for them to bear. Moreover, Yangzhou and Zhenjiang are separated by a river, and the measures are clearly different. Since soy sauce has been sold throughout the country, soy sauce from Jiangbei, made with Huai salt, has been flowing in. The suffering of Zhenjiang merchants is already difficult to express. If we impose harsh regulations that do not exist in other provinces, how can they maintain their business? Therefore, we are reporting the situation and requesting that you review it. We hope that you will consider the plight of the Zhenjiang soy sauce merchants and approve the revocation of the original punishment and grant exceptional leniency. We eagerly await your instructions. Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce seal.

Local News

Old Ningshao Steamer and Beian Steamer Collide in Huangpu River This Morning. Ningshao More Severely Damaged, Beian Slightly Damaged. Both Parties Report to Navigation Bureau, etc. 96

The Northern Shipping Company's Beian steamer, with a capacity of 3,585.89 tons, unloaded coal in Shanghai and set sail from the Zhonghua Wharf at 4:00 a.m. yesterday, heading to Nanjing to load cargo. At around 5:00 a.m., it arrived at the Huangpu River near the Waibaidu Bridge, i.e., the Lujiazui River surface. At the same time, the Ningshao Company's Old Ningshao steamer, replacing the New Ningshao, was operating the Ningbo route. The steamer, with a capacity of 2,642 tons, was fully loaded with passengers and cargo and arrived in Shanghai from Ningbo yesterday morning. It arrived at Lujiazui at 5:00 a.m. The Ningshao steamer saw the Beian steamer departing and sounded its horn three times. The Beian steamer did not change its course, resulting in both steamers being unable to avoid each other when they approached, leading to a head-on collision. Due to the excessive force of the impact, the bow of the Ningshao steamer was completely destroyed. The iron plates on both sides were completely dented, and a large hole was punched in the right side of the bow. Both anchor holes were also destroyed. The bow of the Beian steamer was also damaged on both sides, and a large hole was also punched in the right side. Although the Beian steamer was empty, the extent of the damage seemed to be less severe than that of the Ningshao.

Report by Shipowners

After the incident, the Ningshao steamed to the wharf, and passengers disembarked and unloaded the cargo. The Beian steamer was also unable to leave the port and changed to anchoring at buoy No. 21, awaiting inspection and repair. According to the report of the Ningshao steamer's owner, when his ship was sailing in front of the Yisong Shipyard, he saw the Beian steamer coming. The Ningshao sounded its horn once in advance, but the Beian did not respond. The Ningshao sounded its horn again, but the Beian still did not respond. On the third sounding of the horn, the Beian responded once. At that time, the steamers were approaching each other, and the Ningshao quickly sounded its horn twice, and the Beian also responded twice. However, the Beian did not change its course. The Ningshao steamer steered to the left, and the Beian also steered to the left, making it impossible to avoid each other, resulting in a collision and causing this disaster. The owner of the Beian steamer reported that when he saw the Ningshao, he first sounded his horn three times, then sounded his horn three times again, and told the Ningshao steamer that the Beian had stopped. At that time, the tide was rising rapidly, and the Ningshao was proceeding very quickly with the tide. The Beian was sailing on the Puxi side. When the steamers approached each other, they collided. The truth of the matter needs to be determined by impartial persons and ship inspectors.

Both Suffered Great Losses

The bow of the Ningshao steamer was almost completely destroyed. The outer iron plates of the bow were broken, the keel was also damaged, and all other internal decorations were damaged. It is completely unable to sail. According to people in the company, the loss will be at least 16,000 to 17,000 yuan. As for the Beian steamer, because there are no cabins, the loss is relatively light, but it cannot sail either. It must be repaired in the factory before it can sail.

Various Reports of Inspection

After the Old Ningshao unloaded its cargo and passengers, the company telegraphed the Jiangnan Shipyard to send a tugboat to the Ningshao Wharf. At around 3:00 p.m., the Shao steamer was towed to Gaochangmiao, preparing for major repairs. However, in order to inspect the losses, the Ningshao Company reported to the Maritime Affairs Bureau and the China Ship Insurance Federation, requesting that technicians be sent to inspect the ship. At the same time, Yisong, Ruirong, and Jiangnan Shipyards were also requested to send engineers to Gaochangmiao at 8:00 a.m. this morning to survey the damage and then carry out major repairs. The Beian steamer was also reported by the Northern Company to the Maritime Affairs Bureau and foreign insurance companies, requesting that personnel be sent to buoy No. 21 to inspect it before repairing it.

Ningbo Route Suspended

The Ningshao Company's Shanghai-Ningbo route New Ningshao steamer is currently undergoing routine repairs, and the Old Ningshao steamer is temporarily used as a substitute. The regular routes on Monday, Wednesday, and Friday have been suspended because the Ningshao steamer was damaged and cannot sail without major repairs. Therefore, the Ningbo route steamer that should have departed yesterday was temporarily suspended. Most of the passengers going to Ningbo went to the French Concession and changed to the Taikoo New Beijing steamer, so the New Beijing departure last night was crowded with passengers, which was rare. The Ningshao will have to suspend another route tomorrow. Yesterday, the company telegraphed Ningbo to inform them that the New Ningshao steamer can be repaired and leave the factory next Monday and officially resume sailing.

Tianjin-Tanggu Area: Record of Two Maritime Ships Colliding. Xintai Hits Tongli 97

The Tongli steamer of the Tongcheng Company in this port set sail from Tanggu to Tianjin on the afternoon of the 15th of this month. When it was sailing near the fourth section of the port surface, the Xintai steamer of the Xintai Steamer Company followed behind. It came closer and closer. However, the Xintai was traveling too fast, causing the stern to run aground on the north beach, and the bow suddenly turned to the left, pushed by the tide, and collided violently with the Tongcheng steamer, causing damage to the right side of the Tongli. He has reported this to the Shanghai Insurance Company yesterday, requesting that both parties conduct an inspection to clarify the truth.

International Convention on Load Lines for Ships: Our Country Officially Joins 98

Our country's participation in the International Convention on Load Lines for Ships was submitted by the Ministry of Communications to the Executive Yuan for review. The Executive Yuan ordered the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Navy to draft their opinions and forward them to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation and approval. The National Government then ordered the Executive Yuan to forward them to the Ministry of Communications, which forwarded them to the local Maritime Affairs Bureaus. The details of the process are as follows:

Ministry of Education Submits Request to Executive Yuan for Review

The Ministry of Communications believes that more than 30 countries around the world have joined the International Convention on Load Lines, and our country did not join it in the past because the shipping industry was not yet developed. Now that the country is planning to develop the shipping industry, the mutual relations between international navigation will inevitably become closer. In order to facilitate international navigation and protect the safety of life and property at sea, it is felt that it is necessary to join this convention. The ministry has attached a translated version and the original text of the convention and submitted them to the Executive Yuan for review, and asked the Executive Yuan to forward them to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation. After receiving the report, the Executive Yuan ordered the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Navy to review it.

Ministry of Finance and Ministry of Navy Draft Opinions

After receiving the order, the Ministry of Finance ordered the Customs Administration to forward the convention to the General Inspectorate of Customs for review. Subsequently, the General Inspectorate submitted its proposed opinions to the Ministry of Finance, arguing that training personnel should be prioritized before considering joining the convention. The Ministry of Navy also drafted its opinion, arguing that it should be joined immediately. The Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the Ministry of Navy then held a meeting to review the two opinions. It was decided that the convention could be supported in principle. The Executive Yuan approved the report of the Ministry of Finance and others and presented it at the 211th meeting, requesting the Legislative Yuan to review it, and instructed the Ministry of Communications and the Ministry of Navy to prepare for the technical personnel who inspect the load line.

Legislative Yuan Approves Government Order for Compliance

The Legislative Yuan approved the advice from the Executive Yuan and first handed the case over to the Foreign Affairs and Commercial Law Committees for review. According to the report, it seemed that it could be joined. After a joint meeting discussed and resolved to approve the review report, it was submitted to the 25th General Assembly for approval. The Executive Yuan was notified. The Executive Yuan then submitted it to the National Government for record and formally notified all countries of its accession to the convention. At the same time, the government ordered the Executive Yuan to forward the order to the Ministry of Navy and the Ministry of Communications, which forwarded it to their subordinates.

According to the Central News Agency, the American International Trade Association holds an annual meeting every year, gathering representatives from cities and states across the country, economic experts, government commercial officials, and inviting foreign celebrities to participate in order to discuss the obstacles to American foreign trade and how to improve it. Whether we will organize a study group or send personnel to participate is still under consideration.

Implementation of Flour Inspection from September 1st. Imported Flour Must Be Inspected Before Import 100

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry has decided to implement flour inspection from September 1st. After that, imported flour in Shanghai must be reported to the bureau for inspection and be qualified before it can be declared for import. The Inspection Bureau yesterday issued the detailed rules for the implementation of flour inspection as follows: Article 1: These detailed rules are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 18 of the Commodity Inspection Law (hereinafter referred to as the Law). Article 2: All flour imported from abroad shall, before customs declaration, fill in the inspection application form to the local Commodity Inspection Bureau (hereinafter referred to as the Inspection Bureau), together with the inspection fee, and apply for inspection. A certificate shall be issued to those who pass the inspection before they can be declared for import. Article 3: The Inspection Bureau shall, upon receiving the inspection application form, immediately send personnel to select samples. The sampling methods are as follows: 1. Select 8 bags for 100 bags or less, 15 bags for more than 100 bags but less than 1,000 bags, and 20 bags for more than 1,000 bags but less than 10,000 bags. Each bag shall contain 4 liang (125 grams) of the market system. 2. Mix the goods mentioned in the previous paragraph together, extract 2 jin (1,000 grams) of the market system (divided into four bottles) and seal them with the sampler's seal. One bottle shall be used for inspection, one bottle shall be kept by the applicant, and two bottles shall be stored in the bureau for reference. The rest shall be sent back on site. 3. The samples shall be selected by the sampler, and the applicant shall not designate them. 4. After the sampling is completed, the sampler shall add a seal to each package and issue a sampling certificate. The sampling certificate shall be numbered by the Inspection Bureau and signed and issued by the sampler. Article 4: The order of inspection shall be based on the order in which the inspection application forms are received, and the procedure shall be completed within two days after sampling. Sundays and other holidays may be extended accordingly, but when necessary, work may be carried out as usual. Article 5: The standards for qualified flour inspection are as follows: 1. Properties: White or slightly yellow, without any peculiar smell or mold, and without any parasites. 2. Impurities: Do not contain the following impurities: (1) Stone powder, chalk, alum, copper sulfate, and other substances that are harmful to health. (2) Poisonous plant seeds and flour ground from wheat that has developed ergot disease. (3) Other starchy powders. 3. Fineness: The amount that cannot be sieved through a sieve with 42 holes per square centimeter shall not exceed 0.20%. 4. Moisture: Not to exceed 15%. 5. Crude fiber: Not to exceed 0.50%. 6. Ash content: Not to exceed 1%. Article 6: The Inspection Bureau may evaluate the grade of flour according to the inspection results of the previous article. The grading standards are as follows: First grade: Color: Pure white; crude fiber: below 0.20%; ash content: below 0.50%. Second grade: Color: White; crude fiber: below 0.35%; ash content: below 0.75%. One grade: Color: Grayish white or slightly yellow; crude fiber: below 0.50%; ash content: below 1%. Article 7: After the inspection is completed, the person in charge of the inspection shall sign the inspection application form and issue a certificate or inspection form in accordance with the provisions of Article 1 of this law. Article 8: The Inspection Bureau shall affix a mark on the packaging of qualified flour. Article 9: The validity period of the flour certificate is three months, but it may be extended for three months if necessary. Article 10: In accordance with the provisions of Article 12 of this law, for any flour that has passed the inspection, a re-inspection may be applied for to the Inspection Bureau during the validity period of the certificate by submitting the original certificate. An application for re-inspection of unqualified flour shall be made within 14 days of receiving the notice of unqualified status, and the original inspection application form shall be submitted. However, the Inspection Bureau may reject the application if it deems that re-inspection is not necessary. Article 11: When re-inspection of unqualified flour is allowed, the Inspection Bureau shall send another person to select samples and supervise the inspection. Article 12: When qualified flour is transported to various places in batches, a batch transportation report form shall be filled out and submitted to the Inspection Bureau together with the original certificate for verification and exchange for a batch transportation certificate. Article 13: When flour that has been inspected and qualified by Bureau A is transferred to the location of Bureau B, a transit report form shall be filled out and submitted to Bureau B together with the certificate issued by Bureau A for verification. If it is confirmed that the original packaging is consistent with the certificate, a release note shall be signed on the original certificate and exempted from inspection. However, if any discrepancies are found, the inspection shall be carried out again. Article 14: In accordance with Article 13 of this Law, if a certificate is requested to be reissued or exchanged, the Inspection Bureau may re-inspect if it deems that there is no sufficient reason. Article 15: Flour that is re-inspected in accordance with the preceding two articles shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 2 of these detailed rules. Article 16: If the certificate is lost during the validity period, in addition to reporting the loss and applying for a replacement certificate in accordance with the law, the original certificate number and the circumstances of the loss must be published in a prominent local newspaper for more than two days, declaring it invalid. Article 17: The Inspection Bureau may formulate supplementary measures for the implementation of flour inspection, but it must be submitted to the Ministry for record. Article 18: These detailed rules shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Businesses Hope Loan Committee Considers Their Difficulties; Flexible Loan Procedures; Small Loans to Be Granted with Flexibility; Repayment Deadline Extended to One Year 101

The Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee held its eighth meeting on the 20th. The attending committee members were Cai Zengji, Du Yuesheng, Chen Guangfu, Bei Songsun (replaced by Chen Guangfu), Song Ziliang, Wang Yansong, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Zuoting, Zhang Peikun, and Xi Demao, totaling ten individuals. During the meeting, they reviewed twenty-two applications for small credit loans that had been investigated and reviewed. After reviewing each case, they were divided into three categories: "approved for loan," "approved with reduced loan amount," and "rejected." The approved applications were processed accordingly. Eight applications were approved for the full amount requested, eleven were approved with reduced loan amounts, and one was rejected. Two applications were approved pending the guarantor's written confirmation of guarantee. The total amount of small loans approved was over 27,000 yuan. It is reported that recently, there has been a steady stream of applications to the committee. The completion of the application forms is mostly guided voluntarily by the Lixin Accounting Firm on Ningbo Road, and errors have gradually decreased. Therefore, if industrial and commercial firms wish to apply for loans but are unsure of the form completion procedures, they should first consult the Lixin Accounting Firm for guidance to facilitate the process. In addition, to show consideration for the difficulties of industrial and commercial businesses applying for loans and to thoroughly implement the initial intention of relief, the committee also proposed at this meeting: (1) to grant small loans to semi-industrial, commercial, and small businesses with flexibility to provide widespread relief; and (2) to modify the repayment period for small credit loans to a maximum of one year. Both proposals were approved and will be submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval and implementation. The original text of the proposals is recorded as follows:

Flexible Lending for Small Loans

(1) Proposal to grant small loans to semi-industrial, commercial, and small businesses with flexibility to provide widespread relief. The original text of the proposal states: "It is noted that the restrictions in the loan regulations were too strict during the seventh meeting of this committee. A study on flexible measures within possible limits should be conducted to facilitate implementation." After discussion, it was decided that Chairman Cai and representatives from various banks would conduct a detailed study and submit the results for discussion at the next meeting. On the 15th of this month, Zengji convened representatives from various banks to jointly conduct a study. It was generally agreed that since the committee had already proposed to the Ministry of Finance a plan for flexible guarantee methods, the most difficult point for applicants would be resolved upon approval. It seemed unnecessary to amend the other points in the regulations. However, for semi-industrial businesses applying for loans under 500 yuan and small businesses applying for loans under 200 yuan, if the guarantor is found to be reliable and creditworthy, even if their own financial strength is insufficient, flexible handling and lending should be considered. Furthermore, applicants with sufficient financial strength and the ability to repay the loan may be granted a waiver of security to align with the initial intention of widespread relief. The results of the joint study are now submitted for discussion to determine if they are appropriate. Proposer: Chairman Cai Zengji."

Modified Repayment Period for Small Loans

(2) Proposal to modify the repayment period for small credit loans to a maximum of one year. The original text of the proposal states: "It is noted that according to Article 9 of the ten principles promulgated by the Ministry of Finance regarding the repayment period for small credit loans, repayment should be made at the end of the term according to market practice. In reality, the latest loans issued must be repaid by the end of this year, leaving loan applicants with only a short period of four months to use the funds, which is not very beneficial. Currently, most applicants request a repayment period of one year or eight months. In consideration of practical circumstances and to thoroughly implement the initial intention of relief, it seems appropriate to modify the repayment period for small credit loans, referring to the regulations for mortgage loans, to a maximum of one year. With such a longer term, borrowers can benefit more and avoid the difficulty of tight credit at the end of the term. This would also contribute to market stability. It is submitted for discussion to determine if it is appropriate. Proposer: Chairman Cai Zengji."

Request to Waive Stamp Tax on Checks; Original Letter from the Bankers Association to the Ministry of Finance 104

The Shanghai Bankers Association is submitting another case requesting the amendment of the Stamp Tax Law. The previous reply from the Ministry of Finance was not adopted. However, the industry believes that the stamp tax on checks greatly hinders the circulation of negotiable instruments and the turnover of funds. Therefore, they are submitting another request to the Ministry of Finance to maintain the old policy and allow for exemption from stamp tax. The original text is recorded as follows: "Submission regarding the earnest request to maintain the old policy and temporarily postpone the stamp tax on checks. A reply was received from your ministry on July 23, Tax Zi No. 6380, regarding the case submitted by the association and others requesting the amendment of the new Stamp Tax Law, with attached opinions. After careful reading, it is noted that the item regarding checks was approved by your ministry in 1929 for exemption from stamp tax. The new Stamp Tax Law now classifies this type of negotiable instrument as an important document and changes it to a stamp tax of two cents per item. This is already a light levy among the taxes. It can be seen that the legislation has profound implications. We should not discuss it again. However, the current financial situation is severely depleted. Encouraging the circulation of credit instruments is an urgent priority. Even if the market has one more turnover chip, it can indirectly reduce the outflow of social funds and contribute to the country's economic construction. Furthermore, although the tax liability for checks belongs to the drawer, most ordinary depositors have not yet developed the habit of using checks. Adding this burden will not only hinder the implementation of the function but also make existing customers who understand the effectiveness of checks and issue more checks inevitably reluctant to use them and worry about penalties for missing stamps. Therefore, for various reasons, check users will inevitably tend to use passbooks for payment. The number of checks will decrease accordingly, and cash movement will inevitably increase. Those who are cunning will benefit from the convenience of checks but also worry about the stamp duty and may turn to foreign banks. In theory, Chinese and foreign parties are the same and subject to the same penalties, but in practice, there are many complications, which have a considerable impact on financial security. After repeated consideration, the association believes that the time is not yet ripe for stamp tax on checks. The other points requested for amendment in the original opinion have been explained and should be followed. Therefore, we are submitting another request to your ministry for approval to maintain the old policy and temporarily postpone the stamp tax. The new Stamp Tax Law will be implemented on the first day of next month. Before it is finalized in this city, we should also request that all inspection agencies be notified to handle the inspection of stamp tax on checks with leniency to avoid disputes. We deeply hope that your ministry will approve this request and we will be grateful for your convenience."

Xu Shiying, Chairman of the Disaster Relief Committee, recently went north to inspect the Yellow River flood disaster. He returned south on the 20th and arrived in Beijing last night. In addition to reporting the Yellow River disaster situation and undertaking disaster relief, he plans to come to Shanghai on the 24th to attend the first standing committee meeting of the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Flood Relief in Various Provinces to be held on the 25th. The association also received a telegram from Xu Shiying in Bian reporting on the disaster situation. The excerpt is as follows: "To the President, Vice Presidents, Directors, Deputy Directors, Secretaries-General, and Gentlemen of the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Flood Relief in Various Provinces: I departed from Kaifeng this morning, traveled along the south bank of the Yellow River embankment, and passed through Lanfeng, Kaocheng in Henan, Dongming, Changyuan, Puyang in Hebei, and Heze and Juancheng in Shandong, totaling seven counties. I did not reach the Dongzhuang gate. The ground level in Kaifeng is lower than the river level, and the future danger is worrying. The Kaocheng Civil Levee has been raised and a protective embankment has been built, so there should be no problem. The Yellow River disaster in Hebei Province only affects Dongming, Changyuan, and Puyang, three counties. The disaster area is relatively small. The disaster victims number about 200,000 people. However, houses and farmland in the river beach have been flooded, and there is deep water accumulation inside the embankment. Most of the victims have moved to the embankment, and the disaster situation is dire. At the junction of Hebei and Shandong provinces, the Liu Zhuang embankment is facing a dangerous situation. The river affairs bureaus of the two provinces are working on reinforcement. The storage of materials is being prepared. Heze and Juancheng counties are the most severely affected areas in Shandong Province. More than 10,000 disaster victims are gathered on the embankment. Their faces are pale and their bodies are thin. The situation is unbearable. The Dongzhuang No. 1, 2, 3, and 4 gates have been silted up and cut off. However, the No. 5 and 6 gates have merged into one and are 800 zhang wide. The main flood is over 200 zhang wide. The large flows from both rivers have entered the breach. 90% of the people in Shandong want the breach to be closed urgently. Chairman Han and Committee Chairman Li Yizhi are holding a procedural meeting on closing the breach in Dongzhuang in a few days and have reported to the Yuanhui. However, it is heard that there has been unprecedented heavy rain in Ningxia. It is expected that around the date before, the disaster area in the lower reaches of Henan and Shandong will not be large, but the disaster situation will definitely worsen, which is very worrying. Shiying returned to Bian late at night and is now returning to Beijing to report to the Zhenwu Committee. Committee Chairman Xu Shiying. Mao Si 4."

After the New Stamp Tax Law Takes Effect, Old Books Do Not Need to Be Stamped Again; City Chamber of Commerce Replies, Stating Reasons and Requesting the Ministry of Finance to Issue an Explanatory Order by Telegram 110

After the new Stamp Tax Law takes effect on September 1, the stamp tax for ledgers will be 2 jiao per book per year, which is different from the current Provisional Regulations on Stamp Tax, which is 1 jiao per book per year. The City Chamber of Commerce recently received inquiries from various industries asking whether old ledgers that have not been used up and continue to be used after September 1 should be stamped with an additional 1 jiao. The City Chamber of Commerce immediately provided detailed instructions based on the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Stamp Tax Law and telegraphed the Ministry of Finance requesting an explanatory order. The letters and telegrams are recorded as follows:

Telegram to the Ministry of Finance

"To the Ministry of Finance, Nanjing: According to the Stamp Tax Provisional Regulations, the effective period of stamp tax payment on continuing to use ledgers should be until the end of the year's commercial closing date or the end of its designated accounting year and does not need to be fully stamped with 2 jiao according to the Stamp Tax Law. This is a natural interpretation based on legal principles. Inquiries from various places sometimes have doubts about this. Please, your ministry, issue an explanatory order to avoid suspicion and misunderstanding. Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce."

Reply to the Silverware Industry Letter

"Direct reply: We received your letter on the 20th of this month asking whether ledgers used before September should be fully stamped with 2 jiao after the new Stamp Tax Law takes effect. This matter can be discussed in two layers: (1) According to the principle of not applying the law retroactively, the Stamp Tax Provisional Regulations are not governed by the new Stamp Tax Law that takes effect on September 1. (2) The issue of the effective period should be discussed. Although the Stamp Tax Provisional Regulations have been abolished after the Stamp Tax Law takes effect, the effective period of stamp tax stamps affixed to ledgers that have not been used up according to the Regulations should be until the end of the year's commercial closing date according to Article 10 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Stamp Tax Law. The tax rate effect of the Regulations on the ledgers has not disappeared. There is no need to stamp again at this time. To the Shanghai Silverware Industry Association."

Guangxi Finance Department Imposes Additional Yarn Tax; Yarn Mill Association Appeals for Exemption 112

The Chinese Yarn Mill Association sent a letter to the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating: "We respectfully inform you that we received a letter from the Wuzhou Flower Yarn Industry Association stating that the province held a business tax last year, considering cotton yarn as a necessity for people's livelihood. Therefore, the business tax for selling cotton yarn was halved compared to other industries, levied at 2 per mille. Now, the tax rate has been revised, and all industries are taxed at 6 per mille, and the halved rate for cotton yarn has also been abolished. Our industry's burden has suddenly increased by two-thirds. All donations and fees required for cotton yarn from Shanghai to Guangxi have reached more than 20 yuan per package. Current sales are already sluggish, and it is impossible to increase costs further. We earnestly request that you transfer the request to reduce the levy to 2 per mille or halve the rate to avoid collapse. Cotton yarn sales have been declining in recent years. Fortunately, Guangdong and Guangxi provinces have purchased more. The cost of transporting Shanghai yarn to the south has already been large. If the business tax of 4 per mille is suddenly increased, the cost will increase again, and sales will inevitably decrease. Manufacturers and yarn merchants in Guangxi Province will suffer, and even Guangxi's tax revenue may not increase. Therefore, we earnestly request that you transfer the situation to the Guangxi Finance Department and ask them to continue to levy the Wuzhou cotton yarn business tax at the old rate. If an appropriate increase is necessary, please follow the previous method of halving the tax rate to benefit yarn sales and maintain the factory industry. Please examine and approve this request."

Song Municipal Government Asks to Repair the Seawall; There Are Also Collapsed Parts in the Baoshan Section 114

The tide outside the Wusong mouth has been high recently, and the sky is often hazy, which is a sign of storms. The seawall in the Songbao area, in its important places, has been repaired last year, and the seawall is still considered solid. However, the sections such as the Five Peaks Mound in the Baoshan section were attacked by the storm tide in June 1933. The piles and stone beaches in each section collapsed a lot, and the soil was loose and sinking. When it was repaired last year, due to funding reasons, several projects in the area were not repaired in the end. The tide has risen greatly in recent days, and the damage to each section is even greater. Now, Yan Fenlou and others from the Baoshan Tangdong have telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Government to quickly allocate the 100,000 yuan of seawall funds listed in the provincial budget for 1935 and estimate the construction to avoid major disasters. It is learned that the Tanjiabang North section of the seawall in the Wusong District of this city was originally a temporary emergency project during the hurricane in 1933. After two years, the Jiangchao has washed away and there are many defects. If it is attacked by a violent storm, there may be a risk of collapse. Yesterday, Wu Song Municipal Commissioner Yin Gongtian, together with gentlemen Gu Zhouchao and Zhang Panshi, went to inspect and immediately prepared a document to submit to the Municipal Government to order the Bureau of Public Works to send personnel to repair it quickly to avoid danger.

Sino-Foreign Relief Association: Report Received on the Hubei Flood Disaster 117

The Sino-Foreign Relief Association on Jen Kee Road recently received the first report on the Hubei Sino-Foreign Relief inspection of the Hankou to Caidian Xiang River flood disaster. Excerpts are as follows: (1) Conditions along the route: since the association's vessel sailed upstream, the north bank from Tuoluokou and the south bank from Qinduankou and above were indistinguishable from the sky and water, with no shore to be found. The willow tips floating on the water were like duckweed, and the exposed tile ridges were like floating gulls. (2) Residence of the victims: on the south bank, from Heshan to Ma'anshan, the victims' shelters were either closely packed or simply mats on the ground beneath the sky. This information was obtained through telescopes, so it was not possible to capture videos. (3) The state of Caidian: this city belongs to the second district of Hanyang and is known for its prosperous commerce, unmatched by any other. Currently, the entire city is flooded, with boats traveling through the main streets, all businesses suspended, and the people showing signs of hunger. (4) Causes of the disaster: the city is located by the Han River, with the Xiangyongti and other embankments acting as a barrier in the rear. On July 12th, the Xinzhakou Sanhe and other embankments of the Xiang River successively collapsed. The Han River, being at a higher elevation, rushed in, and the Jiudouti and others also collapsed due to the breach of the Lanjian dike. Therefore, within a few hours, the water reached the eaves. According to the watermarks, although the water level has dropped by about five feet, the city's houses are still half-submerged in the water, and the area outside the city is a vast expanse of water, all fertile farmland. (5) Victims awaiting relief: due to the sudden flood, goods and food in the city were washed away, the autumn harvest is hopeless, and the death toll is estimated to be over 500. The people are all without food and awaiting relief. The farmers are especially hoping for the distribution of autumn seeds. The Hubei Relief General Association of the Commercial Red Swastika Society has allocated several thousand yuan to purchase and distribute food, but this is insufficient due to the large number of victims. A second report was received after inspecting the fifth district of Hanyang and Xinkou Town, on the Nang River flood: (1) Causes of the disaster: the district borders the Han River in the front and is traversed by the Fu River (Xinkou). The town is located at the mouth of the river, on the extreme south, and relies on the Honghu dike of Hanchuan to block the western water. Unexpectedly, on July 7th, the Hong dike collapsed, and Kangjia Yuan in the fifth district was the first to be submerged. Subsequently, due to the expansion of the Yuan, it breached the Kang dike and converged with the Fu River. Moreover, the high water level of the Han River hindered its discharge, causing it to rush horizontally into the Yihe Tiesuo and other Yuans, flooding the entire district. Although the water level has now dropped by five feet, except for the dikes where the victims can set up shelters, the rest of the district's fields and houses are still half-submerged in the water. (2) The situation of the disaster: Xinshi had been heavily flooded, but has now receded, leaving muddy streets and a foul odor. The district had already harvested 80% of the spring crop this year. The stored grain was completely submerged within a day due to the sudden flood, and the autumn harvest is also hopeless, resulting in a very tragic situation, with hungry people grabbing food. (3) Inspection of the disaster area: today, together with the district chief and others, we took a boat up the Fu River to inspect the breached dikes in areas such as Yihe Tiesuo and Kangjia Yuan. Countless houses were collapsing into the water. Moreover, the entire district has no high ground. Not only do the people have no place to settle, but there are also no burial sites for the floating corpses that are being salvaged. Photos were taken to document the tragic situation.

Maigen Road Freight Depot Extends Free Storage Period 121

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways Administration, in order to facilitate merchants, has specially revised the free storage period and storage rates of the Maigen Road Freight Depot. They have agreed with the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Authority that for goods transported to Shanghai by the administration within one month, the two railway administrations will provide free storage for one month. The Tianjin-Pukou Railway also expressed its approval and the following regulations were established: (1) From August 15th to September 14th, within this one-month period, the free storage period for goods shipped from various stations of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway to the Maigen Road Station will be temporarily changed to one month (originally seven days). Beyond this limit, the exceeding portion will still be charged according to the regulations. (2) For this free storage period, excluding the original seven days, the Tianjin-Pukou Railway will bear 50% of the storage fee. To facilitate settlement with Tianjin-Pukou, the Maigen Road stationmaster should promptly list the actual storage dates of each batch of goods in detail when the free storage period ends in mid-October and submit it to the responsible section for processing. (3) The quantity of goods eligible for one month of free storage is limited to 15,000 tons. If this amount is about to be reached or the capacity of the Maigen Station's warehouses is about to be full, the stationmaster should promptly report to the responsible section for approval. (4) When goods arrive, the Maigen Station should conduct a particularly detailed inspection. If there is any dampness, it should be immediately reported to the responsible section for approval. (5) During the same period (from August 15th to September 14th), goods shipped from various stations of this railway and other connecting railways to the Maigen Station will also receive special preferential treatment, with a free storage period of 15 days, without tonnage restrictions.

To Avoid Competition, Tobacco Retailers Sign an Agreement 125

The Shanghai Tobacco Retailers Association has repeatedly received reports from members that the price of foreign goods has recently increased sharply without decrease, and that many stores are being opened by people from other industries, resulting in competition and disputes, leading to operating losses and maintenance difficulties. They have already realized this and are willing to unite and formulate an agreement, requesting the association's permission to jointly comply with it in order to maintain business development. Based on this, the association held a meeting and passed the revised agreement. Yesterday, it dispatched personnel to distribute notices to the city inside and outside the South Gate, and solicited unanimous participation from the industry to affix official store seals on the agreement to show credibility. Next, it will be promoted in Zhabei and the three concessions of England, France, and the United States. The articles of the agreement are excerpted as follows: (Article 1) This agreement is based on the general outline of the wholesale agreement formulated by this association, with the purpose of reorganizing the industry, unifying prices, and safeguarding the public welfare of the industry through voluntary unity. (Article 2) The publicly agreed price list will be distributed by the office, and all members of the industry must abide by it and not disrupt it. (Article 3) Those who agree to join the agreement should each pay a security deposit, divided into three grades: Grade A, three yuan; Grade B, two yuan; and Grade C, one yuan. The total amount will be deposited into a reputable bank and kept by four publicly elected persons. The office will issue a certificate, which can be used to pick up goods from tobacco companies and wholesalers. The aforementioned certificate must not be lent to others for use, otherwise it will be revoked. (Article 4) If a member who agrees to join the agreement violates the agreement, and it is reported secretly or found to be true after investigation, the security deposit paid by the store will be confiscated (the confiscated funds will be disposed of separately). For Grade C, after the first offense, the security deposit will be confiscated and another five yuan will be paid. For the second offense, the security deposit will be confiscated and another ten yuan will be paid. For the third offense, the security deposit will be confiscated and the certificate will be revoked. For Grade B, after the first offense, the security deposit will be confiscated and another ten yuan will be paid. For the second offense, the security deposit will be confiscated and another twenty yuan will be paid. For the third offense, the security deposit will be confiscated and the certificate will be revoked. For Grade A, after the first offense, the security deposit will be confiscated and another fifteen yuan will be paid. For the second offense, the security deposit will be confiscated and another thirty yuan will be paid. For the third offense, the security deposit will be confiscated and the certificate will be revoked. If, after the first offense, the second security deposit is not paid, the tobacco companies will be notified to cancel the industry's benefits, and for those without industry benefits, the certificate will be revoked and they will not be allowed to pick up goods from wholesalers. (Article 5) For those who have not joined the agreement, personnel will be sent to solicit their participation in the agreement. Those who withdraw halfway should request the tobacco company to stop supplying them with goods and the wholesaler to stop supplying them with goods. (Article 6) Newly opened stores must join the agreement and obtain a certificate from the office. Without a certificate from the office, they will not be allowed to pick up goods from tobacco companies and wholesalers. (Article 7) Members who join the agreement must be responsible for supervising each other. If there is any behavior that disrupts market prices, and it is reported or secretly reported and found to be true, the store's security deposit will be confiscated, and the reporter will be given a reward of three times the amount (the reward will be paid from the security deposit paid by the offending merchant). (Article 8) Members who join the agreement will be issued badges by the office and may go out at any time to investigate the prices of other members. Those being investigated must not refuse. (Article 9) If a member who joins the agreement uses gifts as a promotion or similar disguised gifts, it will be considered selling at a low price, and the store's security deposit will also be confiscated. (Article 10) If a member who joins the agreement sells at a low price while peddling outside, they will also be punished according to the agreement and the security deposit will be confiscated. (Article 11) The security deposits paid by members who join the agreement will be the responsibility of the elected custodians, deposited in a bank, and not allowed to be used for other purposes. (Article 12) If there are any matters not covered in this agreement, they may be decided by means of a meeting, but must be approved by more than half of the members present in this district.
