Little Men (22) 196

— Originally Written by Ms. Louisa May Alcott; Translated by Zheng Xiaocang (Zonghai)

Who is "Too Fat"? We have already said above that his original name was George Curry. He was first spoiled by an indulgent mother, because she fed him too many candies, later he became ill, and too weak to work hard. By the time he was twelve years old he had become a pale, bloated child, sluggish, irritable and lazy. A friend advised her to send him to Plumfield, where he soon became refreshed, because here, sweets were rarely allowed, exercise was compulsory, and lessons were so interesting. "Too Fat" followed this gradual persuasion and unknowingly improved, until his worried mother was surprised, and fully admitted that the air in Plumfield did have some incredible magic.

Thorny was a sharp and cunning boy, he was sent to this school simply because it was a "reform" one. Many people might think of him as a clever and astute boy, and even though these qualities are praised by Americans, Mr. Bhaer did not approve of the conduct by which he exhibited these qualities, and felt that his premature sophistication and his love of money were a big problem, no lighter than Dolly's stutter or Dick's hunchback.

Ned as like other billions of fourteen year old boys, was all legs, stumbling, crashing. His family called him "Clumsy," often afraid he would trip over a chair, or turn over chairs and tables, or knock over small objects. He often boasted that he could do this and that, but rarely did so in practice to prove his words. Lacking courage, he also could not avoid gossiping, habitually bullying younger children, and flattering older children. We cannot simply say he was bad, but he was definitely one of the misled.

Page 16

Shen Bao National Products Weekly

Words of Contribution

Chinese People Themselves Must Rise Up First for Chinese Goods 197

— Yang An

Mr. Arnold, the senior commercial attache of the United States in China, I have talked to him several times, and he always said the benefits of Chinese goods and the infinite hope of Chinese goods. This time he spoke at the Shanghai Rotary Club, and his words were even more thorough. Mr. Yinliang's abridged translation of this newspaper on August 18th made people feel infinite emotion and infinite anticipation after reading it. He said: "The reason why national products cannot compete with others is not only because they cannot be improved and are not managed with new methods, but also because the Chinese themselves do not use them first, and foreigners will naturally not use them. I can give a few examples: A few weeks ago, I went to Guangzhou with the American Economic Mission. The banking community held a welcome reception in a Chinese hotel, and the tea used was entirely foreign tea. The Guangzhou Chamber of Commerce used Chinese tea when welcoming them, but they drank it in a foreign way, using excellent black tea and diluting it with milk, completely losing the flavor of Chinese tea. Someone suggested that the mission find ways to promote Chinese tea, so we told him to promote Chinese tea in Chinese society first. Sometimes in Chinese hotels, Chinese trains, and Chinese clubs, it is simply impossible to find any Chinese tea. If you don't let foreigners drink Chinese tea and let them taste the benefits of Chinese tea, how can you get them to buy Chinese tea?" These words are so straightforward and thorough, so Mr. Yinliang summarized: "To get foreigners to use Chinese goods, first improve Chinese goods and get the Chinese to use them themselves." As far as I know, the current general unpromising and shameless Chinese people still believe in and enjoy using foreign goods. A certain organization openly said: We have never used national products. I don't know what the motive is for this perverse attitude? Recently, the Greater China Rubber Factory has created automobile tires, and the products can be said to be on par with foreign products. Many highways are enthusiastically adopting them. I heard that a certain association, no matter what, refuses to adopt them. Has this element that hates national products forgotten that he is Chinese? Alas, if the Chinese themselves do not trust and love to use national products, what hope is there for the country? Rubber tires are just one type of national product. In addition, such as food, drink, use, and wear, if everyone can take out their conscience and gradually improve them first, and then use them themselves, then there will be a glimmer of hope for the future of national products.

The Thrift Movement and National Products 198

— Xuan Wan

The high level of national worship of foreign goods and the cultivation of extravagant lifestyles are the main reasons for my country's huge import surplus over the years. At the same time, we can work hard to promote the thrift movement and the promotion of national products, which is the only trend to save the current crisis.

As everyone knows, since the commodities of imperialism broke through our closed-door policy, on the one hand, Western material civilization has gradually been introduced into the country. At the same time, the goods of several industrially advanced countries first arrived in the cities of our country and began their dumping tactics. As a result, we, who had backward production and had never seen machine-made goods, were greatly tempted, and the result was that in the lives of our people, whether spiritual or material, they tended to be westernized and extravagant, and a large number of foreign goods salesmen were produced, creating the foundation for the collapse of the domestic economy and the bankruptcy of industry and commerce over the years.

Let us take a closer look at the people in today's society. In the current situation, how rampant are those who live a Westernized and extravagant life? In general, the bourgeoisie must wear imported clothes, eat European food, live in Western houses, and travel in cars. Even cosmetics and stationery must be foreign. But then look at the middle and lower classes? They are also affected by the upper class. Although a salaried class who relies on twenty or thirty dollars to maintain their lives, their husbands must also wear suits and leather shoes, and their wives must perm their hair, paint their eyebrows, dye their nails, wear cheongsams, and high heels, as if they are not enough to be proud of themselves without this. However, on the other hand, the import surplus has increased sharply, and there is a shocking leak every year, and the country is becoming weaker day by day. Is this not their gift? Moreover, even from their personal point of view, have we not often heard of "unemployment" and "suicide" recently? The reason is nothing more than the result of too extravagant family life, economic pressure, business failure, and the fall of personality, leading to this final fate.

Therefore, I deeply feel that under the current enthusiastic promotion of the slogan of national products, it is necessary to work hard to promote the thrift movement at the same time. I remember that the New Life Movement has included the national product movement and thrift to save the country in the same category, and we must follow it closely. Recently, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and many groups have also called for the promotion of the thrift movement. This kind of opinion and trend is very correct. In this time of national poverty and exhaustion, I hope that everyone will not return to the Westernized and extravagant life, and instead find a way out for the future of national products!

The Chinese People Should Firmly Remember National Product Trademarks 199

— Du Yun

Since recently, we can say that we are in an era of commercial warfare. If you want your own goods to sell well and earn other people's money, the first thing is to pay attention to the authenticity of the goods and meet the needs of the times. But once you have achieved your goal, you are still afraid of others imitating and counterfeiting. Therefore, adding a trademark can help you recognize each other. Since the Chinese people have advocated national products, the manufacturing output has been increasing day by day, and almost all daily necessities are available. And each goods has a registered trademark for identification. Therefore, when Chinese people buy domestic goods with patriotism, remembering the trademarks of domestic goods is also a more convenient method.

Trademarks are commonly called brands. When you mention a certain brand of goods, you will think of the quality of that brand. For example, when you mention "Guben Soap," you know that it is effective in removing dirt, durable, and does not damage clothes; when you mention "Triangle Brand West Lake Towel," you know that it is soft and absorbent; when you mention "Invincible Brand Tooth Powder," you know that it can clean teeth, strengthen teeth, and has a fragrant smell; when you mention "Double Ten Brand Toothbrush," you know that it is comfortable for brushing teeth and does not shed bristles; when you mention "Lihe Brand Washbasin," you know that it is beautiful and durable. Remembering the trademarks of national products is a clear proof of trusting national products. If the Chinese people can all do this, are we still afraid that national products will not sell well?

The above are just a few famous national product trademarks. If we go further and remember the national product trademarks of various necessities, then when you don't have time to buy them yourself, even if you send servants or commission agents, you only need to explain the goods and trademarks, and there will be no mistakes. Even some stores that are used to selling foreign goods will find it difficult to use their tricks to pass off foreign goods as national goods!

To implement the method of firmly remembering national product trademarks, in the family, parents should naturally take the lead. Whenever you buy a certain product, in addition to remembering it yourself, you must also point out to your children what this thing is, what the brand trademark is, and which domestic factory it is produced from. You may not remember the factory name so much, but you must let them firmly remember the brand. In schools, teachers should naturally take the lead, especially in primary schools, because middle school students can already identify them themselves. Or sometimes hold tests and ask them to say the trademark names of domestic goods, or during games and exercises, such as when performing "Wearing the Dragon Gate," where everyone usually reports a flower name or bird name, now ask them to report a domestic product trademark name, which is also quite interesting. In short, there are plenty of ways to remember national product trademarks, only that the Chinese people work hard to implement them!

A Good Example of Promoting National Products 200

— Sun Choucheng

This time, the New Pharmaceutical Industry Association, due to the issue of registered medicines, elected Zhou Bangjun, Xu Xiaochu, and others to go to Beijing to personally present their opinions to the Department of Health. I also went along. Qin Moxiao, a reporter from this newspaper stationed in Beijing, invited us to visit the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum, took the opportunity to visit the Tan Yankai Tomb, and then went to Linggu Temple to visit Xu Pengfei, Chairman of the Committee for the Construction of the Cemetery for Fallen Soldiers. Mr. Xu is from Wuxing, Zhejiang, and was a close friend of the martyr Chen Qimei. He is quite straightforward in nature. When talking about the issue of promoting national products, he cited a story to prove the enthusiasm and perseverance of the Japanese, which is worth recording. It is not that I am increasing the ambition of others and diminishing my own prestige, but the fact is so. I hope that compatriots who are addicted to using foreign goods will emulate each other after reading this. Then, even if the national crisis is serious, it may not be possible to save it. Otherwise, it is useless to advocate it verbally, and if you cannot put words into action, the current silver is limited, and there will always be a day when it runs out. Even if strong neighbors do not force me with guns and cannons, I will die of economic exhaustion, just like a person suffering from anemia. Even without an external infection, I will die of my own accord. Mr. Xu said: During the late Qing Dynasty, I had already changed my attire. When I was with Mr. Sun Yat-sen in Japan, one day I planned to make a set of spring suits. I went to the market to look at the goods and saw that most stores were priced at 28 yuan. Later, I discovered a store that was priced at only 20 yuan, and the material was the same. The lower price was even more refined than the higher price, so I ordered a set in this store. On Sunday, when Japanese friends gathered, I saw that the material they were wearing was coarser than what I was wearing. When asked about the price, they all said 28 yuan. Comparing it with what I was wearing, they also admitted that it was cheap and good. When asked where I bought it, I told them the address and store number. They all said that I was planning to buy it at this store because the material in this store was foreign goods. What we are wearing is Japanese goods. You are Chinese, so naturally you choose to buy from cheaper people. If we also don’t use domestic goods, then our domestic woolen industry will never improve, and the outflow of rights and interests will be unimaginable. Even if we know that domestic goods are more expensive and inferior than foreign goods, we should also promote them with pain. If you want beauty and cheapness, making a set of suits for 20 yuan will completely flow into foreign countries. Now, buying a set of domestic suits for 28 yuan, each person spends 8 yuan more, which is a small amount, but calculated across the country, the amount is very large. The domestic woolen industry has a surplus due to its wide sales, so it will gradually improve in manufacturing, and there is no fear of not being able to achieve the four words "cheap and good" and compete with foreign goods. Therefore, we are willing to pay a high price to buy goods of inferior quality, although it is painful for a while, but the hope is endless. When I heard what they said at the time, I deeply admired their broad vision. More than 20 years later, every time I see Japanese goods that have improved and are cheaper, I often think of the scene of the conversation at the time. Therefore, I made up my mind not to use foreign goods from that year on. Now I am used to it and don't feel that Chinese goods are unusable. However, fashionable friends who are influenced by European culture often think that Chinese goods are not as good as foreign goods in terms of quality and efficacy, and the price is not cheap, so they are unwilling to use them. If everyone doesn't use them, the sales volume will not be large, and even if they don't go bankrupt, they will only barely maintain themselves. How can they hope to improve? I hope you will announce this intention in the National Products Weekly to help promote national products. I admire his enthusiasm and specially express it to tell the readers.

Promoting National Products Depends Entirely on Conscience 201

— Yi Yi Guan Zhu

Originally, when a person does things in the world, no matter what he does, he must rely on his conscience to do it well. Is it only "promoting national products" that is so?

However, this article of mine is written for "National Products Weekly". Therefore, I will specifically talk about "promoting national products".

We know that "promoting national products" is not something that started today, it has actually been going on for a long time. However, the results are getting worse and worse! Now we don't have to ask for "foreign goods" not to have a "trade surplus", we only need to ask for the number of "foreign goods trade surplus" to only decrease and not increase, and that is still impossible! Let alone "national goods" being able to have a "trade surplus"? In this situation, "promoting national products" is simply empty talk! It has been like this for decades up to today. How can we not blame the national economy and people's livelihood for getting worse every day? Alas! This... This... This... What is the reason for this? Thinking carefully, this is entirely a matter of each person's "conscience"!

Because, a person with a "conscience" can do anything well. "Promoting national products" is also like this. If you have a "conscience", then you say "promoting national products", you must be sincere and will not deceive people. Naturally, you can say it and do it. Otherwise, "promoting national products", no matter how good it sounds on the mouth, is unfortunately insincere. What you wear; what you eat; what you drink; what you smoke; and everything you use, are still all "foreign goods" behind your back! This kind of self-deceiving behavior is really untrustworthy. If a person is untrustworthy, what "conscience" does he have? It is only because he has no "conscience" that he will sell "foreign goods". It is only because he has no "conscience" that he will purchase and use "foreign goods". How can we not be bad if we promote "national goods" like this? Therefore, I want to nag here and say: "Promoting national products depends entirely on conscience". I just want to hope that everyone will take out their "conscience" when promoting "national goods" in the future!

The Plan to Make Newspapers from Straw (Part 1) 202

— Tian Xu Wo Sheng

The machine for making newspapers is not a problem. It's like cooking a small dish. It only depends on the skill of the cook. There is no need to order an electric stove or gas stove. What is already available, such as the Pinglian machine of Longzhang Tianzhang, can be used to make both sides smooth. As for the reel type, the machine itself comes with a reel, so there is no difficulty. The only difficulty is the pulp problem. My brother and I have been making pulp and paper from straw for more than ten years. It can be said that we have already succeeded. However, it is not cost-effective to buy straw in the city. One yuan only gets about three dan. Therefore, it cannot compete with foreign newspapers for cheapness. But making pulp in rural areas can save the cost of transportation. Its cost is more than two-thirds cheaper. Moreover, it is not only for making newspapers, but also for selling grass pulp abroad. Let’s take Jiangbei as an example.

According to a friend, straw in places such as Dongtai and Yancheng can be bought for eight dan per yuan. Wheat straw is twice as much. However, shipping it to Shanghai is very uneconomical because its value is too cheap and the ship price is more expensive than the grass price. According to the proportion of shipping cotton, a ship can load more than 300 dan. The Chuan donation package costs 90 yuan net. The journey takes one month. If you ship straw without paying taxes, the ship price can be cheaper, about 60 yuan. If you calculate it for 300 dan, the cost of shipping each dan has already cost two jiao. Adding the grass price of one jiao and two and a half fen, it is the same as the price of one yuan and three dan in Pudong, Shanghai. However, in places such as Chongming and Haimen, the price of straw is only two and a half dan per yuan, but the scale used is actually the same as the lime kiln scale. Each jin is equivalent to 22 liang of the balance. Then each yuan is equivalent to more than 340 jin, which is also equal to one yuan and three and a half dan in Wuxi. Because I am aware of the difficulty of shipping from Sichuan, I feel that making pulp locally in Dongtai and other places is a great source of profit that can be developed and is most economical. Because making pulp from straw yields one ton for every 4,000 jin. Each ship can load 20 tons, which is equivalent to loading three ships of grass into one ship. The freight can be saved by two-thirds. If each ship costs 60 yuan, the shipping cost per ton is only two yuan. Adding the grass price of five yuan, the total is only seven yuan. The lime used can be brought back on an empty ship. But if the water feet are not suitable, sodium sulfide can be used instead. Each barrel of 60 pounds costs 3.5 yuan and can make 1.5 tons of grass pulp. Then the 20 tons of grass pulp used only needs 14 barrels. The total board is less than 6 dan. The cost of shipping is also calculated at two jiao per dan, which is only 1.2 yuan. The total statistics for each ship is 20 tons. Including the grass price, the cost is only 211.8 yuan. Selling 14.4 yuan per ton, you can get 288 yuan, which is a net profit of 76.2 yuan. According to my humble plan, if the rural cooperative promotes a small workshop, with 40 people operating each, they can produce 5 tons per day. If 160 people work, they can load one ship per day. They can produce 600 tons per month and sell them for 8,640 yuan. Deducting the advance payment of 40 yuan each to 160 people, totaling 6,400 yuan. The shipping cost is 1,800 yuan. Lime or sulfur is 1,544 yuan. The total is 3,984 yuan. The remaining 3,656 yuan is obtained. After deducting 10% of the cooperative's expenses, the remaining amount is 3,200 yuan, which is 20 yuan per person. Including the advance payment of 10 yuan, they have already received 30 yuan. The total grass required is 24,000 dan. If divided among 160 people, each person produces 150 dan of grass per month. Originally selling 8 dan for one yuan, the income is only 18.75 yuan. Now they get 30 yuan. The monthly living expenses per person can be 11.25 yuan more, which is enough for the food of two old and young people. Although there are only 160 operators, if each person's 20 yuan is enough for the food of five people, it is enough to prevent 800 orphans from starving. If you are afraid of a shortage of straw, you can calculate it by the area of the field. Each mu can average 10 dan. But with 30,000 mu of land, it is enough for them to operate all year round. If each person farms 40 mu with two people, then there should be 1,500 farmers. Now the number of workers is only one-tenth. If they operate during the slack season, then each person operates for one month each year, which is more than enough. However, if you operate at one time, the investment required is about 50,000, which requires the assistance of a bank. As for sales, the total amount of 7,200 tons is only enough to supply one cardboard factory. The total price of the grass pulp sold is 7,200 tons, which can get more than 100,000 yuan. When the cooperative takes 10%, it has already obtained 10,000. To pay the bank's interest, calculated at 1% per month, return it monthly, calculated at 8,000 yuan per month. In the first three months, it is treated as accounts receivable, and the interest is 1,500 yuan. By the fourth month, 24,000 yuan has been paid off, then the interest is only 260 yuan. In the fifth month, another 8,000 is returned, then the interest is only 160 yuan. In the sixth month, another 8,000 is returned, and the interest only needs 80 yuan. In the seventh month, the entire amount is paid off. The total interest paid is only 2,000. There is still 8,000 yuan left, which can be used to pay the members, directors, supervisors, and other rewards.

Slight Loosening of Foreign Short-Term Loans; Rise in Prices of Fractional Coins; Slow Progress in Silver and Money Trades 205

In previous years, Shanghai's business, especially during the peak season of new autumn for department stores, saw frequent use of silver funds. However, this year, much of it has been affected by the slow adjustment of the financial industry. Spot goods are difficult to purchase, and no one pre-orders goods. Therefore, although the market is in a boom season, its idle state is no less than that during the slack season of hot summer. The repayment of financial public debt this time has not yet been fulfilled, and the headliners of its counterparties are unevenly distributed. Those who are in short supply have no ability to repay, and even those who have surplus funds are still waiting and seeing. Because of this mutual concern, the market atmosphere is even more stagnant. Yesterday, the price of foreign short-term loans in the market was 18 cents in the morning and noon, a slight decrease of 2 cents compared to the previous day, but the headliners still did not add water, and the easing of the loan market remained the same. Most of the warehouses did not accept funds. Free Talk

Depictions of the Ocean 217

— Bai Lu

Because I am someone who likes the ocean, I have a special fondness for texts that depict it. I often think that the beauty of the ocean changes along with the state of mind of the observer. Sometimes it's a loving mother, sometimes a sleeping infant, and sometimes it seems like an all-consuming tyrant or devil. Some people say that the sea holds many secrets that it can tell people things they don't know. When I face the ocean or read texts that depict it, I don't feel that this is an exaggeration at all.

In the past, what I loved to read the most was the section describing the ocean in D'Annunzio's "The Triumph of Death," where a dying person listens to the howling of the sea waves under a starlit sky and is aroused by all sorts of bizarre hallucinations. Although it takes the form of a novel, reading it is just like reading a richly imagined, eloquently worded prose poem. Burton Rascoe said that his writing is imaginative and descriptive, and this can be seen in this text. The roar and weeping of the sea, the bewilderment of dreams, the threat of death, and the solemnity of the twilight that appears at dusk, all weave together in the lines into a most enchanting and mysterious picture. He writes of the harmonious music of the sea slowly unfolding under the pure lilac sky of July. He also uses personification to write of the sea's anger, jealousy, humility, dejection, ridicule, comfort, groaning, and prayer, all kinds of behaviors. His descriptions are ornate, not stingy in using all the new words and adjectives that can be used.

In contrast, Gorky also uses personification to depict the sea, but it is all simple. He uses very few strange words, only sketching a few strokes like a watercolor painting, and a vivid image appears on the paper. In works such as "Malva" and "The Birth of a Man," he uses the most economical and effective relief-style techniques to depict the sea. He seems to see a few key points of the beauty of the ocean, focusing on expressing these key points and abandoning the dross that is not worth writing about, so the beauty of the scenery is concentrated within the scope of these few sentences. He writes "the sea is laughing" and "the sea is surging with cheerful waves," this "healthy laughter" that makes people yearn is also a symbol of the state of mind of the giant in this period of rebirth. Simplicity, purity, and strength are precisely the unique advantages of new literature.

The excellence of some older writers' techniques for depicting the ocean is still something we cannot forget. For example, Pierre Loti's "An Iceland Fisherman," which was recently translated, writes of the sea as mysteriously lovely and at the same time frighteningly frigid; in the looping depictions, it reveals a kind of Nordic atmosphere. Each chapter is like a gradually unfolding picture scroll. Writing about the sea, he did not forget to write about the people on the sea, so his pen not only conveys the struggle between people and natural forces, but also another aspect of the sea as seen from the psychological perspective of people, writing out the entire color taken from the outside world, but reflected in the inner world, while at the same time giving the mood the same tone.

I once saw a book by Ibner Nas titled "Our Sea," in which the activities of a female spy during the European War were written about, with many strange things in the sea, which was written in a rather monotonous way. In addition, what I can't bear to let go of is Lafcadio Hearn's essay about watching the sunrise on the beach, which takes great pains to describe the rising sun, the waves and sails under the rising sun. Although the environment written about is not much different from what Gorky wrote, the mood is completely different. Gorky's description of the sea is full of life-giving, romantic exaggeration, while Lafcadio Hearn only uses the tone of a lyric poem to calmly narrate the fairytale-like realm of a love song, bringing a kind of hazy and tactful poetic interest. The former is a "wild cry" for "natural force," while the latter is just the work of a meditative poet lingering on the scenery. Life determines the work, and there are such cases.

From ancient times to the present, I don't know how many authors have spent their energy on depicting the ocean, and there's no end to what could be said, but what we demand now is not a poet who is intoxicated by the wonderful scenery of the ocean and engages in mysterious meditation, but a singer who can see the "sprouts of new life" in all great things, to sing and depict the "angry tide of the Chinese sea"!

Analysis of Word Formation 218

— Wang Fuquan

Regardless of using "phonetic symbols," National Language Romanization, or National Language Latin Script, the defining, reforming, and creating of "words" is a common, fundamental issue.

Here, we will attempt to analyze the formation of words. (Of course, this is just a starting point.)

(I) Same Meaning—Wang Yinzhi's "Jing Yi Shu Wen," Volume 32, "Tongshuo Xia," "Parallel Placement of Two Characters in Classics and Commentaries with Same Meaning": "Yinzhi respectfully notes: In ancient exegesis, repetition was not avoided; often, there were two characters placed in parallel, with the same meaning above and below. Interpreters who divide them into two meanings miss the point. For example, in the 'Tai Xiang Zhuan,' 'The sovereign thereby regulates and completes the way of heaven and earth, and assists and guides the suitability of heaven and earth.'… 'Regulate' and 'complete' have the same meaning… 'Assist' and 'guide' have the same meaning. In the 'Sui Xiang Zhuan,' 'The gentleman thereby retires to rest in the evening.'… 'Banquet' means 'peace,' and 'peace' and 'rest' have the same meaning…" Examples include: roads, obstruction, residence, dispersal, fatigue, inversion, guests, fear, and collapse.

There are also two words with the same meaning that, when combined into one word, either retain their meaning or have their meaning changed. For example, the word 目 (mu), can mean eyes, as in "clear and cool eyes"; it can also mean the main point, as in the "Transmission of the Lamp" "To study Chan, one must make great use of the eyes in response to the moment."

(II) Similar Meaning—Combining two words with similar meanings into one word can be divided into two categories: one in which, after being combined into one word, the meaning includes both of the similar meanings; the other in which, after becoming one word, the meaning has changed.

Examples of the former include: poetry and song, ballads, appearance, etiquette, rules, laws, and banquets.

Examples of the latter include: firewood and rice, referring to daily necessities; pen and ink, referring to poetry; Zhu and Mo, referring to things needed for writing; paper and pen, referring to contracts; clothing and hats, which can refer to officials; crowns and tassels, which can refer to the ruler; strings and bamboo, referring to music; shields and spears, referring to war; wood and stone, referring to things without awareness ("Mencius," "Living with wood and stone.") (The above examples are what is called "synecdoche" in rhetoric.)

(III) Opposite Meaning—Examples include: big and small, left and right, good and bad, male and female, buying and selling, lending, victory and defeat, much and little, reward and punishment, yin and yang, deep and shallow, life and death, long and short. This type can also be divided into two categories: one includes both meanings, and the other changes the meaning. However, even the category that includes both meanings has a slight change in meaning. For example, "Decide a victory or defeat" can be interpreted as deciding whether you lose and I win, or I lose and you win; it can also be interpreted as fighting a battle. For example, "Return several taels of gold and several dozen samples, be they many or few, to the teacher," "many or few" can be interpreted as "however many taels…" or it can be interpreted as "a total of several taels…"

The latter category includes examples such as "A decisive showdown," which means a decisive victory or defeat. "If something long or short happens" means if a person has a "three longs and two shorts" (i.e., death). "I just want to borrow from a friend" here only means to borrow, not to lend. "Now is a moment of survival or extinction," which means when about to perish. "Go through a crisis" means it is a time of emergency.

Here, there is another type of formation, where the meanings of the two words being combined are neither similar nor opposite, but rather opposing. Examples include: east and west, rules, water and fire, father and son. After being combined, the meaning has completely changed. "Unable to distinguish east and west" means not knowing the direction (east and west can also be interpreted as "things"). "Not understanding rules" means the rules have become etiquette. Water and fire refer to "the mutual restraint of things," and father and son "contain the meaning of succession."

(IV) Reduplicated Words—Examples include: papa, mama, older brother, younger brother, wife, grandma, gradually, often, only, frequently, haha, playing, walking, sitting, everyday, just now. The first line of the first poem in the "Book of Songs" ("Guan Guan cry the ospreys") is an example. Li Qingzhao's "Sheng Sheng Man" contains the famous examples of "searching, searching, seeking, seeking, cold, cold, clear, clear, miserable, miserable, sorrowful, sorrowful, grieved, grieved."

(V) Due to Alliteration—Examples include: seemingly, hesitation, displacement, mountains and rivers, melancholy, ancient and modern, addition and subtraction, rules, yin and yang.

(VI) Due to Rhyme—Examples include: wandering, confused, absurd, hazy, leisurely, graceful, vague, water and fire, old and young, good and ugly.

There are many examples of the fifth and sixth categories. (Regarding words formed due to sound and rhyme, there is one point that should be mentioned in passing: Zhang Taiyan's "One Character Heavy Sound Theory." "For example, 'shuo jiao' in the ren radical has 'jiao yao,' yao is the original character, and jiao is the borrowed sound character; why not also create qiao? This shows that the character yao also has the two sounds of jiao and yao.")

(VII) Category Name Plus Distinguishing Word—A category name plus a distinguishing word can be divided into two categories: one, above the category name; two, below the category name.

Examples of the former include: scientist, writer, warlord, academic bully, dictionary, thesaurus, banknotes, pawn tickets, big dog, small dog, chartered rickshaw puller, car driver, white horse, black horse.

Examples of the latter include: tears, eyeballs, electric light, telephone, girls' school, female doctor, essay, literature.

(VIII) Original Word Plus Initial or Terminal Particle—Adding an initial particle, such as agong (grandfather), apo (grandmother), ashū (uncle), azie (older sister), ayi (aunt), or lao xiong (old brother), lao bo (old uncle), lao da (oldest), lao er (second oldest), lao Zhang (old Zhang), lao Wang (old Wang).

Adding a terminal particle, such as chuangzi (window), kuzi (pants), dianzi (cushion), daozi (knife), shanzi (fan), zhuozi (table), erzi (son), nuzi (daughter), qizi (wife). Also, such as ping'er (bottle), pen'er (basin), niao'er (bird), yaozi'er (to ask for money), hai'er (child) (there are many terminal particles using "er" in Hangzhou dialect). Also, such as mutou (wood), quantou (fist), bitou (nose, also called bizi), dingtou (nail head, also called dingzi), zhitou (paper), guantou (can), niutou (button).

(IX) Street Slang and Suffixes—This is similar to but different from the seventh and eighth categories. Prefixes, such as anti-revolution, anti-Semitism, not comprehensive, not prosperous. Suffixes, such as idealization, scientification, generality, necessity.

Regarding the formation of words, it can roughly be divided into the above nine categories.

Here, there are also a few miscellaneous points that I will try to write down.

The reduplicated words in the fourth category mentioned above can be reduplicated into four "characters," such as nannan nü nü (men and women), mingming baibai (clearly and plainly), hucong mangmang (hurriedly), lulu xùxù (continuously), hehe qiqi (harmoniously), tuntun tutu (hesitantly), laolao xiaoxiao (old and young).

There is a kind of so-called "supplementary explanation," as described by Wang Zhong in "Shuxue," "Releasing Three Nines," such as three appointments, three dismissals, three battles, three victories, nine deaths, nine oxen, nine lands, nine heavens. Also, such as four seas, ten directions, full marks, everything.

The above is just something written down casually; of course, I plan to write about it in more detail in the future.

Evening 219

— Luo Hong

In any season, I often love the evening the most. People probably all love the morning: when you are still wearing soft pajamas, standing in front of the window with a sleepy expression, facing the bright sky, watching one or two thin clouds floating lazily past, or watching three or five small birds flying gracefully in the morning breeze, that is truly the most leisurely thing. If you wake up from a dream, look at patches of azure sky through the cracks in the curtains, and listen to the vague sounds of the city coming from afar, then reach for a favorite book by the pillow to read, or hum a favorite song idly, you will definitely experience a lot of fun in between. However, for those of us who bear the burden of life, where would we have such leisurely days? Every day, we just hope to get through the day quickly, letting the burden of life carry us and squeeze ourselves under the giant wheel of life. Only in the evening do we give ourselves a sigh of relief, sit lazily in my chair, watch the branches outside the window being blown by the evening breeze, watch the setting sun hanging on the corner of the wall, and indulge in a few comfortable breaths. All dreams of hope also float up at this time, and we get a little self-deprecating comfort for the burden of life.

Speaking of evening, I love the times of summer and autumn. The summer evening is especially beautiful, it is so refreshing and gorgeous that it makes people feel cool and brilliant. When you wear a light, thin shirt, stand under the shade of a tree, or by a short fence, and let the evening breeze play with your short hair and the corners of your clothes, that is much cooler than sitting in a cafe eating shaved ice. And there is also the blue sky, with the clouds dyed by the setting sun, the bright colors and the changing postures, watching them gives a gentle pleasure. At this time, no matter what sorrow or joy is forgotten, I often think that only nature is the most beautiful. As for the autumn evening, I love its tranquil colors and the slightly sad atmosphere. It makes people easily think of the past and leisurely bring up many longings. At this time, I sit in my chair, sighing, as if blowing away the burdens of the day's life, silently looking at the faint sky, watching flocks of birds skimming diagonally past my window.

Rain 220

— Libo

Many people love rain. "Night Rain Xiao Xiang" has become a famous line from ancient times, "Rain hitting plantain leaves" is also said to evoke a clear and poignant parting sentiment, "Rain washing pear blossoms" can even make people imagine the tragic beauty of "pear blossoms with rain," and "under the rainy window" has indeed become a blessed land for many pure and lofty people.

But I deeply detest rain. Rain is the most unfeeling thing. It dampens the light, diminishes the strength of the flowering branches, and further isolates the roads of human interaction. It is like pouring tears, but these tears are devoid of affection, coldly without a trace of warmth or saltiness; they are not human.

Every night, when I am bitten awake by bedbugs, I feel cold and disgusted when I hear the sound of rain. I turn on the light, but immediately turn it off again; I originally wanted to get up and catch a few bedbugs, but because I hate to see the rain, I don't catch the bedbugs either. I think, bedbugs make people disgusted, but they still know human blood; and they openly risk death to be the enemy of humanity, and they still have the courage to live. Being bitten by them, being unable to sleep because of it, is better than watching the color of rain.

The rain falls bleakly, hitting the small window. I remember just now when I turned on the light, I glanced and saw that the white window curtains were wet from the leak in the roof, and tomorrow, a yellow stain will be left on the wet area. Then, I thought in a roundabout way about the countless swollen corpses on the turbid waters of a dozen provinces.

Rain is hateful. But it is so insensitive that it doesn't even realize that it is hated, and it keeps dripping incessantly, dripping on the roof, floating on the windowsill, making a chirping, shameless sound.

Even snow and ice are good; snow has whiteness, and ice has piercing coldness, both are better than tepid rain. As soon as a person gets wet in the rain, they can only feel endless mustiness.

"But rain is indispensable. Rain is a necessity of daily life."

Precisely because it is a necessity of daily life, it only has this function, and nothing else, which makes it even more annoying! People don't just spend their daily lives.

If someone asks: There is a crown inlaid with luminous jewels, but wearing it requires enduring a month of torrential rain, and there is a fierce fire, a raging volcano, and in the mountain there is a ring that was worn by a beautiful woman who was burned to death and that cannot be melted by the fire, which do you want, to wear the crown in the rain or to take the ring in the fire? I say, go get the woman's ring, get it and be a dead woman's man forever, or fail to get it and be burned to ashes because of it, either is better than watching the gray raindrops in the tepid, loveless, and hateful daily life.

That's how much I detest rain and people who love rain, and I love the sun and men and women who love the sun with the same intense degree.

Love (I) 221

— By S. Sergeiev-Tsensky, translated by Su Ming

S. Sergeiev-Tsensky was born in 1876 and began his literary career at the age of 28. After ten years of literary activity, he fell silent. He did not reappear in the literary world until 1923, when he published his long novel "Transfiguration." During the revolution, he lived in seclusion in the Crimea. He was often isolated from people in the literary world. Critics and readers praised him, and Gorky even called his "Transfiguration" one of the greatest Russian novels of the 20th century. In the current Soviet literary scene, he is not a progressive or active writer. But his works had already earned the praise of many critics and readers before the revolution, and Gorky even called his "Transfiguration" one of the greatest Russian novels of the 20th century. His style is characterized by rich vocabulary and beautiful rhetoric, and he is an excellent stylist. In terms of themes, he is quite similar to Andreyev and Artzybashev, often using death, the cruelty of fate, personal loneliness, and morbid psychological states as his main themes. But in the essay translated here, although the manipulation of fate and the psychology of personal loneliness can also be seen, it already shines with another kind of light. —Note

This was in 1925.

On a large Siberian river flowing into the Arctic Ocean, there was the village of Spassk. There, a young new teacher, recently arrived from Vyatka, was being eagerly stared at by the nineteen-year-old Savaka. Coward—from a small house not far from the school.

The new teacher liked to laugh loudly. On the whole, she was lively, cheerful, and pretty. Her bright red hat suited her black curly hair hanging by her ears very well. When the simple Siberians asked her in the street what her name was, she shook her curly hair and replied, "I—Alyosha."

"What—Alyosha? That's a boy's name," these farmers said, shrugging their broad shoulders.

"That's my name. If you call me Alina, I won't answer, let alone call me Ivanovna."

They called her Alyosha.

When Savaka saw her on the street, he not only began to stare at her eagerly, but also stared at himself eagerly. He did something he had never done before: he examined himself in a mirror.

His face was a very ordinary face. His cheeks were broad and flat, as if they had been slightly ironed. His gray eyes looked out stubbornly from under his eyebrows, and no matter how hard he tried to make them attractive and affectionate, they always looked like two wolves seeing a stranger in their den.

Every day Alyosha passed his small house on her way back from school. One day he plucked up the courage to tell her, moving his lips slowly: "I am—a carpenter. I learned it from my father, he was a good carpenter. But I myself am not that unskilled with mahogany."

"Huh, you yourself are like wood," Alyosha laughed. "Do you want me to ask you to make a dressing mirror out of mahogany, or something else? What do you mean?"

"The advantage is in the work, not in the dressing mirror," Savaka muttered. "It's in you and me."

"What are you saying! In you and me! And who are you? What's your name?"

"My name is Coward," Savaka said, blushing, "but that's not important."

"Coward? What a name!" Alyosha shook her curly hair.

"But that's not important," Savaka replied stubbornly, and then added very softly and wonderfully, "I have fallen in love with you."

Supplement to the Shanghai Shen Bao

Talking Points

Flower Selection to Aid Disaster Relief 222

— Qiong Sheng

Currently, the Shanghai Charity Performing Arts Festival issued a notice to fellow citizens, saying that Shanghai's ten-mile foreign concession is filled with lights and wine, and seeing the crowds at various performing arts venues and the crowded entrances and exits of cinemas, it is known that our Shanghai compatriots are not completely incapable of saving the disaster victims. Therefore, a Charity Performing Arts Festival is specially held. It is said that this "righteous act" can not only be used to entertain the body and mind, but also benefit the disaster victims, which is truly a win-win situation.

Naturally, there are many things that "combine both goods," especially the things under "lights and wine" in Shanghai can be said to be endless. Therefore, in addition to the Performing Arts Festival, there is also the so-called "Flower Selection for Disaster Relief." The ranks of the flower selection include the President, Vice President, Premier, President of the Senate, President of the House of Representatives, and even the Ministers and Vice Ministers of the six departments of beauty, talent, character, and art. Indeed, the number of disaster victims this year and the misery of the situation are such that as long as one has a little compassion, one should show great mercy, not to mention the spirit of treating all people as brothers and sisters, and the fate of the country and the people. However, this good deed has reached the point where it has to be promoted through "flower selection," which makes us on the one hand feel the hard work of the disaster relief officials in planning, and on the other hand feel the lamentable state of the Chinese people's hearts and the pity of economic fatigue.

Why? First, in recent years, our country has been suffering from economic depression and rural bankruptcy, but this has created opportunities for some people to get rich. Therefore, we cannot deny that the current social situation is developing abnormally to a very serious extent. Therefore, when disasters come, many people want to donate generously but have no money to donate, and the so-called some people cannot see the so-called wailing of the disaster victims all over the country. The righteous act of disaster relief has to be sought from the romantic people who frequent brothels when electing the Flower Country President, hoping that they will show compassion during the romantic events, which is a reflection of this situation.

Secondly, people's hearts are extravagant and morality is declining. These phenomena have recently been used by general "defenders of morality" as good topics for "hating the new tide and advocating ancient rituals." Needless to say, the relocation of prostitutes has been greatly prohibited, and even men and women going to school or swimming together have been banned in various places. However, there are not a few of these seemingly moral people who are mixed in the flower bushes. From the promotion of the righteous act of disaster relief to the election of the Flower Country President, it shows what the hearts of those who are concerned about the world are like, and what their "hating the new tide and advocating ancient rituals" is all about.

Geese Returning to the Grass 223

— Cheng Quan

The sunlight shone weakly and feebly on the fields, and it was autumn again. In the distance, on the top of the small mountain across the way, just like the end of last winter, clumps of withered yellow and empty clouds floated around. Those things, like a collection of a kind of depressed atmosphere, condensed in the wilderness and the frighteningly high autumn sky, stubbornly and thickly, refusing to dissipate. At this time, people gradually felt more depressed and gloomy day by day from their previous cheerful mood, and from this they understood that autumn was indeed coming back without any remedy.

At dusk, in the reflection of the setting sun, flocks of geese flew from the north, foretelling a difficult and severe winter ahead. People know this, people have lived through one cruel winter after another, people are familiar with it!

With a deep and mournful cry, the porch of the old house also became gloomy: an old man rested in the broken sunlight, silently smoking, wisps of smoke rising into the air, in the silence, as if thinking about something that he would never understand. Under the eaves, there were still two or three old swallows' nests, but now, a terrible season was coming, the swallows had gone far away, and these dilapidated nests that were left behind also seemed so desolate!

I still remember clearly, in the spring, the roaring and lively season, when the swallows came from the south, the weather was good, and a clear sky for a day ensured that there would be no more wind or rain, and people in a slight but pleasant melancholy, could vaguely remember Yan Shu's lines: "There is nothing to be done about the flowers falling away, but the swallows returning seem to know each other."

But now, it is no longer the swallows that are returning, but flocks of geese.

The fields are still covered with scattered and weak sunlight, and the hometown, when I think about it, should also appear equally desolate, gentle, and pitiful, right? For a life as small as breadcrumbs, drifting aimlessly outside year after year (thousands of miles away!), like hard-working swallows and lonely geese, when night comes, in the deep black days, what is encountered is only the faint dream of a "seemingly familiar" homeland.

Autumn is passing day by day, just like the pages of a book are turned page by page—those withered yellow pages, and what exactly is recorded in them? Are they withered autumn sun and fallen leaves, and the mournful chirping of insects night after night?

The flocks of geese are returning to the south, having gone through such an amazing long journey, crossing such long wilderness and huge rivers, for the sake of merely trying to obtain a little warmer air. Yes, the efforts of such small animals are amazing and admirable, but what about humans, who are called the spirit of all things...?

Drifting, one by one, there are so many, and the cold season is foretelling its arrival, but they are still living in complacency; for the hometown, the warm hometown, it is still some empty and sad memories that are almost hard to believe.

Saying that, it is foolish and cowardly, right?

I once sighed at the departure of the swallows, and now I am feeling the return of the geese—tomorrow's: in such sighs, ordinary time will eventually pass by ordinarily, and silver-white stars will be added to my sideburns.

Come, all withered and cold things, just follow the geese without hesitation! My heart is indifferent and empty, and they can go inside and live.

Yes, the geese are back! It is the autumn of the south, with piles of clouds, an empty Milky Way, a lonely sea, a withered autumn sun... In short, the geese are back.

Night of June 224

— Yago

The night of June is melancholic. Inside this small thatched cottage, it is so quiet, and I cannot help but feel a sense of emptiness in my heart.

The bright moon in the sky shines obliquely on this lush wilderness, casting a milky white silver light, turning the sleeping fields and forests into a silver and beautiful painting.

Although there is no modern clock here, the distant sound of the night watchman’s clapper already announces the third watch. The heat makes me restless and unable to sleep, so I lie awake, lost in reverie.

A mournful cry suddenly arose from somewhere unknown. With curiosity, I quietly listened, but it slowly weakened and subsided. From then on, within no more than five minutes, I heard the same terrifying howl, sometimes so faint, and sometimes bright again.

"Is it the howl of a night wolf? Or a tiger's roar!" But I listened carefully, and it didn't sound like either.

So I got out of bed, found a pair of shoes to wear on the ground, grabbed a black gun from the wall rack with trembling hands, without even checking if it was loaded with gunpowder, and tiptoed out of the door with light steps.

The wilderness unfolded its shadows expansively, revealing a dull tranquility. Dogs curled up under the shade of trees, their strong necks tucked in. The howling subsided, and the evening breeze from the fields sent shivers.

I paced back and forth on the threshing ground with light steps, feeling a sudden sense of anxiety and emptiness in my heart.

Suddenly, the sharp howl came again, and it seemed that I could vaguely hear a final, almost sobbing sound from a woman: "It's bitter!..." The village dogs woke up from their dreams, jumping up as if suddenly struck by a knife, sniffing, raising their heads high, and barking loudly, "Woof! Woof! Woof!"

My nerves began to tremble, and my forehead was damp and prickly with sweat. My hair felt like it was about to

Page 20

stand on end, and I felt a spasm like a malarial patient throughout my body. A terrible thought quickly seized me, making me want to run back into the house regardless. But, after all, I didn't do that. I remembered that I had brought a weapon, and I became bolder.

A force, I don't know when it arose, was bewitching me, so I went straight to the place where the howling was coming from.

Passing through patches of lush green fields, I quietly advanced, my active heart filled with tension and curiosity.

The distant forest, like a lush mountain range, under the silvery sky, reflected shimmering, quivering light.

From the village to this forest, there was originally a wide and open road, with two clear streams flanking the road on both sides. These two streams originated from the mountains and flowed through the fields of the Thirty-Six Villages into the sea. In the past, this stream was regarded as the lifeline of the farmers in the Thirty-Six Villages. When the weather was hot, young people would gather in groups to bathe and frolic here, stripping naked, talking and laughing wantonly, and flirting. The village girls also often took advantage of the market days, using the pretext of washing clothes, to mingle with the young men here.

But in recent years, disasters have occurred everywhere, and this lifeline of the Thirty-Six Villages has been constantly plagued by drowning incidents of persecuted men and women, or hangings on the trees beside the stream, and it has been regarded as a dangerous place. The villagers believe that it is haunted by ghosts and no longer see it as so lovely.

I walked stealthily, and suddenly, under a cluster of trees by the stream, I discovered a blurry shadow wriggling there. Looking closely! I could vaguely recognize that there were three people in total, apparently two men and one woman. The two men were dressed as farmers, dragging and seizing a woman with disheveled hair and tattered clothes, trying to drag her into the forest. The woman desperately clung to a tree root, refusing to go in, sobbing.

I silently thought to myself, "This must be an affair or unwarranted persecution!" I couldn't help but feel angry, and I tightened my grip on the gun, wanting to shout loudly, but when I remembered that the bird gun I had brought was not loaded with gunpowder, I couldn't help but feel flustered, not knowing what I should do: chase after them! Or go back to the village and call for help? I was confused for a moment, unable to decide. But when I calmed myself down for a while and looked at the three characters playing out the tragedy by the stream, they had already run away without a trace, I don't know when.

I felt a sense of depression in my heart and returned to the village.

The next morning, someone went up the mountain to cut firewood and found a strangled female corpse in the stream, but no one knew her name or where she was from.

Less than two months after this incident, an old man, about fifty or sixty years old, with gray hair, came to the village. He was wearing ragged clothes, a bamboo hat, and carrying a bundle on his back. He held aloft a white paper flag with two large characters crookedly written on it: "Seeking Person." He beat a broken gong, calling out in a miserable tone, "Kindhearted and generous people, has anyone seen my Yun'er..." He choked up before he could finish speaking.

Grassroots Work 225

Miners 226

— Yefe

Recently, on the slopes of Huangye Ridge, one can no longer hear the majestic "Miner's Song," but only a string of sighs and curses. The reason is that wages have not been paid for two months.

Other things are not a big deal, but it is the hard-working miners who sweat and bleed who suffer. They all work one day and eat one day. How can you not pay them their wages for several months in a row? So their lives are in panic——

"Damn it, they haven't paid wages for three months. Do they want us to eat coal dust?" A'gou said angrily, taking a break from the winch, wringing the corner of his torn clothes to wipe away sweat. Yinbao glanced at him sympathetically, sighed, and walked from beside the winch to the outside of the shed, inhaling a pipe of tobacco. But his empty stomach remained empty.

"Really, when Shanghai can remit money down, when wages can be paid, those are all lies!" Jinlong couldn't help but interject, roaring, "Lao Er, let's go find the accountant and ask them to calculate our wages. We don't want to work anymore. Anyway, working is starving, not working is also starving. I'd rather starve to death in my hometown..."

"You can't talk like that. What's the use of being irritable? So, we don't work, where else can we go? Isn't it the same everywhere! Don't you see that factories are all laying off workers, reducing wages, and the number of unemployed comrades is increasing day by day? People can't even find a place to work for free. We need to survive now, so we have to endure our temper and work. There's no way around it. In short, blame ourselves for being born into such a world!" Lao Er's voice was already trembling when he said this, but his eyes were almost bursting with blood. However, he finally changed his tone and comforted him, "Although they owe us several months' wages, they will eventually calculate and repay us."

Although Lao Er was comforting them like this, how could he not be angry in his own heart? But what could he do? Several times he went to the accountant to calculate the wages, and he always replied that the general manager had not returned, or that the money remitted from Shanghai was about to arrive that day. But waiting left and right, when a sum of money was remitted, they arranged it for themselves first. How could the workers' share be reached!

Everyone was silent, not saying a word. The surroundings were filled with a tragic atmosphere. A large group of more than fifty people were all squeezed under a not very large reed mat shed. Large piles of coal dust, like small earthen mounds, squatted beside the open space, emitting puffs of gas.

The lever workers, however, were sending coal to the coal storehouse one batch after another——

"They are big bosses, we are workers. Workers eat one day at a time. The whole family has to live. How can they not pay wages for one or two months? What is this?"

"I don't believe what ghosts they are up to. They can't even pay wages, and they still want to run some kind of coal mine?"

"……"

Dang—dang—dang—dang—dang—dang—

The iron plate above the mine sounded, so this group of them swarmed onto the winch, grabbed the levers and turned, turned, lowered one empty bucket after another, and hoisted up buckets of muddy water.

"Ai..." Such a long call echoed in the mine shaft, and the sound waves were very distant and blurry.

"Oh..." The response came from above.

"One zhang seven chi of material section——" The following sentence was climbed up again, so a one zhang seven chi Maosong tree was hung from the bucket. The mine shaft is fifteen or sixteen zhang deep from the ground, and the space in the hole is about four or five zhang wide. More than twenty miners are all working inside; there are five or six carpenter workers, who specialize in managing the splint, scaffolding, and piling. The board jumps are supported at the waist, and people work back and forth on the boards, all in water underneath. There is no air, no light, and the earth gas and a kind of soil moisture suffocate people's brains, almost exploding, but they have to live, so they have to forcibly endure. Although one or two companions always fall ill and are carried back every day, they also pretend not to see it!

Because of less money and smaller scope, many places all adopt local methods, without complete mechanization, so not only does it cost more labor and effort, but also the coal production is very slow.

"Ji—ji—ji—" The dismissal bell rang, so some of them put down from the winch, and some were lifted up from the mine hole, patted the coal dust off their bodies, and dragged their limbs, tired from hunger and hardship, out of the door of the mine house, but everyone's face was melancholy, and there was not a trace of joy. Everyone just lowered their heads and walked silently towards the way home; people, like a group of prisoners released from prison, seemed to be discussing among themselves whether they could get the price of everyone's hard work tomorrow.

News 230

The long-prepared Baijia Singing Society, founded by Wang Yong, Jin Zhi Jing, Huang Jianren, etc., has received very enthusiastic participation since soliciting members. Since preparation to date, it has been nearly two months. The internal affairs have been completely prepared. At the third meeting held the day before yesterday (19th), the righteous decided to hire Cheng Keguang as the General Affairs Director, Wang Tangjin, Zhi Jing Huang Jianren, and Xu Wuyi as the public relations, Zhou Mingyuan as the sound director (cancelled the president director system). It was decided to broadcast a special program on Lili Radio this Thursday from 6:30 to 7:15 first. After selecting a radio station, a long-term program will be broadcast. It is also heard that when the society is formally broadcast, all listeners can enjoy the Baijia cosmetics produced by the German Baijia factory. Details can be heard in future reports.

Movie News

Sketch of New Era Characters 231

— (Tomorrow)

Five, the name Huang Naishuang is very hot, not because she has a similar name with Huang Liushuang, the soulless daughter who fell into a foreign land. As early as four years ago, the Chinese film industry discovered a miracle. The first sound film "After the Rain" appeared very novelly. In fact, the miracle was not this sound film, but the beauty of the heroine Ms. Huang Naishuang in this sound film. Indeed, many fans were fascinated by her slender body and charming face. Unfortunately, after that, she ran to the other side to perform a more realistic drama of life, and had to say goodbye to her enthusiastic audience for a while. Until now, she seems to be a star that has been hidden behind the clouds for a long time, appearing brilliantly in Mr. Wang's film. We believe that Mr. Wang's film is welcomed by the broad masses, and our beautiful little girl has no power!

Six, the New Era Company has two "great men": one is the fat and short Wang Shimu, and the other is the thin and tall Mrs. Chen. Chen Mu is named Zhai Qiqi. She has a gentle temperament, elegant conversation, and broad life experience. She can be a politician, or a virtuous wife and good mother in the family, but she is not interested in those. She resolutely devoted herself to the film industry. She often said that art is a weapon to create a bright society, and she will use the weapon of art to fight against the dark forces in front of her. This spirit is admirable. We wish Ms. Zhai a successful fight.

Seven, everyone still remembers, not long ago, a world's fattest woman came to Shanghai to perform, temporarily satisfying the novelty of Shanghai people. In fact, this is not surprising. If everyone pays attention to the fat appearance of Wang Shimu in Ye Qianyu's cartoon Mr. Wang, then the world's fattest woman would not be so worthy of people's amazement. Of course, this is a cartoon, and people can draw it as fat as they want, but the strange thing followed. When the New Era Film Company was established, to find a female character as fat as Wang Shimu in the cartoon, everyone thought it was impossible, but the day after the advertisement was published, a strange visitor suddenly came to the company. This visitor was Ms. Sang Shuzhen, who later played Wang Shimu in Mr. Wang's film. Her fat appearance does not need my introduction. Everyone must have seen it on the screen. Not only does her identity meet the needs of the characters in the play, but her performance is also very good. This time, when she went to Suzhou to shoot on location, her two big and fat arms were tanned like two purplish-red Jinhua hams. In the play, Mr. Wang was crying loudly that he had no food to eat, Zuo Ming pointed to Wang Shimu's two big fat arms and said: "Why don't you cook these two big hams to eat?" After saying that, everyone couldn't help but laugh.

"Fishing and Killing Home" on the Screen 232

Play within a Play in "Parents and Children"

"Fishing and Killing Home" is a famous historical drama known to women and children in our country. It has now been moved to the screen in the sound film "Parents and Children" by the Culture Film Company, starring Ms. Min Cuiying, a famous amateur actor in Shanghai. Yesterday, a large group of people from the Culture Company - directors, actors, etc., more than 30 people, drove to Wusong to shoot "Fishing and Killing Home". It is a real mountain and real water, with picturesque scenery, a flat boat, white waves soaring into the sky, father and daughter paddling, and both male and female actors wearing specially made ancient costumes, which are full of ancient charm and flavor. In the play, Xiao En and Ding Fu's teacher and apprentice, etc., fought fiercely in the water for eight hours, performing passionately and enthusiastically, which was exciting. Ms. Min Cuiying also sang the "Fisherman's Tears" in the boat, which was colorful and like icing on the cake. The move of "Fishing and Killing Home" to the screen has been prepared by the Culture Company for three or four months. Performed by Ms. Min Cuiying, the pioneer of improving national opera, it is truly an unprecedented initiative on the Chinese stage and screen.

Megaphone Broadcast 233

Zhang Shichuan is preparing for the new work "Peach Blossom After the Calamity" after "Big Family⑥", and Li Pingqian is actively shooting "Love Letter". Yesterday, he convened the actors and staff of the two dramas in the Star Director Department to explain the plot.

After Xia Peizhen completed "Difficult Sisters and Difficult Brothers" by Jixing, she immediately took the lead role in a sound film at the Happy Forest. Now it is said that the central government intends to invite her to shoot a play, which will be produced in Shanghai. At the same time, Xi Jianong, Li Junpan, and Gao Yian are also invited.

The cartoon hygiene film "Resistance" and several other cartoons were specially screened at the Central Health Administration on Monday of last week to commemorate the anniversary. There were many viewers, and all the viewers praised it. The cartoon is the masterpiece of the Wan Brothers, the only cartoonist in China, and it is also the product of the Star Company.

The memorial service for Zheng Zhengqiu was initiated by various groups and is scheduled to be held at Lake Society on Beijing Road on the 25th. It is now heard that Zheng Xiaoqiu also wants to hold a memorial service for his father. It is said that obituaries have been distributed these days.

The Star Tennis Team has now been formally established. Hu Die, Gu Lanjun, Wang Zhengxin, Gong Jianong, Wang Shizhen, He Maogang, He Zhaohuang, He Zhaozhang, etc. are all basic members. If you want to make a friendly match, you can directly send a letter to He Maogang of the Tennis Team of Star Company at Fenglin Bridge.

The New Light Theater is now preparing to start showing films recently. It is said that the first one will be the sound film "Big Family" produced by the Star Company with all the actors, or the full sound "Night Fragrance" starring Hu Die.
